2- The remaining revenues of the above-mentioned companies shall be spent in the relevant subsidiaries of the Ministry of Petroleum, at the discretion of the said Ministry and as the case may be, solely within the framework of the approved budget of the relevant subsidiaries of that Ministry, for the refining, transmission and distribution of natural gas and the maintenance of related facilities, as well as for supplying gas to the remaining cities and villages of the country.
3- The Ministry of Oil is required to allocate the resources of this account, in compliance with the general policies of Article 44 (44) of the Constitution, directly or by using the mechanism of consolidated and combined facilities with authorized credit institutions, solely to finance or provide guarantees for the following projects with the participation of foreign investors (in compliance with Article 80 (80) of the Constitution) or the domestic non-governmental sector:
1-3- Exploration or development of new oil and gas fields or maintenance and increase of production of existing fields in the country with priority given to joint fields, especially increasing the pressure of the joint South Pars gas field.
2.3- Participation in the projects approved by the "Regional Energy Trade Steering Committee"
3-3- Construction, retrofitting, renovation and reconstruction of basic infrastructure required for the storage, transmission, distribution and export of oil and natural gas and processed oil and gas.
4.3- Providing equipment and constructing smart facilities for real-time measurement and monitoring of oil, gas, gas condensate, and oil and gas products.
5-3- Participation in the implementation of plans to optimize and manage the country's energy consumption, especially reducing the imbalance of natural gas and oil and gas products.
4- The resources of this account are transferred to the following year at the end of each year, and fifty percent (50%) of the resources obtained from the repayment of the aforementioned facilities are used to increase the resources of the aforementioned account, and the rest is spent on repaying the debts of the subsidiaries of the Ministry of Oil to the National Development Fund, the Central Bank, and the country's banking network. The use of the resources of this account for any use, including cost credits and the acquisition of capital assets outside the oil and gas fields, is prohibited, except for the above-mentioned cases.
5- In order to coordinate and monitor the proper implementation of this clause, a working group will be formed, headed by the Minister of Petroleum and with the presence of the head of the organization, the Minister of Economic Affairs and Finance, and two supervisory members from the Energy and Planning, Budget and Accounting Commissions, elected by the Parliament.
6- The Minister of Petroleum will be responsible for following up on the approvals of the above working group and ensuring their proper implementation and non-deviation from the aforementioned goals. He is required to submit a report on its performance to the Energy, Plan, Budget and Accounts Committees of the Parliament every three months.
C- The government is required, through the relevant subsidiaries of the Ministry of Oil, to take action to reduce the subsidy for oil and gas (gasoline) in the country's major mines and upstream oil and gas industries, in such a way that the subsidy allocated in both production and sales stages is reduced by ten percent (10%) compared to the base year 1402 in the year of the start of the program implementation and by at least fifty percent (50%) by the end of the program.
The executive regulations of this decree, specifying the examples of major mines and upstream oil and gas industries in the country, will be prepared by the organization within three months of the law coming into force, in cooperation with the ministries of oil, industry, mining and trade, and economic affairs and finance, and will be approved by the Council of Ministers.
Note: Major mines are mines whose oil and gas consumption exceeds five million liters per year.
Productiveness
Article 15 - In order to make the country's oil and gas reserves productive, accelerate the development of oil and gas fields, and improve the government's financial relationship with the National Iranian Oil Company, the following measures shall be taken:
A- The Ministry of Oil is required to enter into separate contracts with the National Iranian Oil Company for fields currently in operation or with a current development contract, in compliance with the laws in the form of long-term contracts, separated by oil and gas fields/reservoirs, including within the framework of the general conditions, structure, and model of upstream oil and gas contracts, with the approval of the Economic Council.
Note - Regarding contracts for fields assigned through long-term contracts implemented within the framework of the general conditions, structure and model of upstream oil and gas contracts that have been approved by the Supreme Council for Supervision of Petroleum Resources by the time this law comes into force, a new contract between the Ministry of Oil and the National Iranian Oil Company will be concluded solely to determine the share and obligations of the National Iranian Oil Company.
The executive regulations of this clause are prepared by the organization in cooperation with the Ministry of Petroleum and are approved by the Council of Ministers.
B- The Ministry of Oil is required to take action regarding other oil and gas fields, with priority given to joint fields and gas fields, using the legal capacities of the National Iranian Oil Company and competitive mechanisms, including issuing licenses as stipulated in the Law on Duties and Authorities of the Ministry of Oil, approved on 1/29/2013, without transferring ownership and sovereignty, to transfer the development, exploration and exploitation activities of the fields to the National Iranian Oil Company and other applicant companies with exploration and production qualifications (as determined by the Ministry of Oil), in such a way that at the end of the third year of implementation of this law, at least two percent (2%) of the country's oil production capacity has been offered to qualified non-governmental applicant companies. This quota is set to increase the country's gas production twice as much as oil.
Note 1- In implementing Article (7) of the Petroleum Law, amended on 22/3/2011, the review and evaluation of the text, financial volume, obligations, product quantity, and implementation time of all contracts subject to this article is the responsibility of the "Supreme Board for Supervision of Petroleum Resources", and the head of the organization is appointed as the secretary of this board.
Note 2- In order to increase the attractiveness of investment in gas fields to reduce the natural gas imbalance in the country, the Ministry of Oil, through its subsidiaries, is authorized, in coordination with the Secretariat of the Supreme Council for Supervision of Petroleum Resources (the Organization), with the participation of the private sector, to take action and issue the resulting products in relation to investment for the development of new gas fields within the framework of gas allocation policies determined by the Ministry of Oil. In compliance with Article Fifty-Three (53) of the Constitution, at least sixty percent (60%) of the income derived from the export of natural gas from these fields, after deducting the share of the National Development Fund and the share of oil-bearing, gas-bearing and undeveloped areas, shall belong to the relevant subsidiary of the Ministry of Oil until the return of the investment made, and the remaining income shall be deposited in the general income account of the government with the National Treasury.
Note 3: Energy-intensive and petrochemical industries, through partnerships with qualified exploration and production companies, are given priority in the allocation of flare gas collection projects and new gas fields. The Ministry of Oil is required to give the aforementioned industries priority in the allocation of natural gas produced from these fields.
Gas production resulting from field development or flare gas collection projects will belong to the aforementioned industries, and these industries are required to settle accounts with the government in accordance with the provisions of the mechanisms mentioned in this paragraph.
Article 16 - In order to manage assets and promote transparency of the assets of executive agencies, the following measures shall be taken:
A- In compliance with Article (21) of the Housing Production Boost Law and the law governing each agency, executive agencies are required to register information on lands, properties, and other immovable properties, including Anfal and acquired properties that they possess as owners, operators, trustees, and representatives of the government, whether they are operated or transferred (with or without ownership documents, leases, endowments, and rights and privileges related to immovable properties, including usufruct rights, easements, and goodwill), in the Comprehensive Property System of Executive Agencies (SADA). Any payment for equipment, maintenance, and other costs for items not registered in the SADA system is prohibited. Failure to implement this clause by the relevant managers of executive agencies is considered a violation.
B- The Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance is responsible for identifying, documenting, and establishing the government’s ownership of the immovable property subject to this article by identifying or designating the operator or issuing an operation certificate for executive agencies, with the exception of Anfal and the instances stated in Article (10) of the Housing Production Boost Law approved in 1400/1/57 and Article 83 of the Constitution. The National Real Estate and Documents Registration Organization is responsible for issuing government ownership documents for immovable property in the name of the government of the Islamic Republic of Iran as the owner, based on the announcement and determination of the Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance. The Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance is recognized as the trustee of government property.
The duties mentioned in this clause are only for items owned by the government and do not include other property in the possession of the government, such as endowment properties. Also, items such as wills that have a specific condition for their use are excluded from the scope of this clause.
The Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance is required to submit a report on the performance of this article to the Parliament every six months.
Other income
Article 17- In order to increase government revenues, the following measures shall be taken:
A- All funds collected as cash fines or penalties for crimes and violations by judicial, quasi-judicial, law enforcement and administrative authorities and state-owned companies in accordance with the laws and deposited in the treasury of the country are considered as general government revenue, and the agencies collecting these revenues do not have the right to use them directly as specific revenue or revenue-expense. The government is obliged to foresee the credit requirements of the aforementioned agencies in proportion to the figures and available credits and within the limits of the government's revenue collection in annual budget bills from the country's general budget credits.
B - Creating new specific income (with the exception of universities, higher education and research and technology institutions) and appropriating existing public income in any way during the implementation of the program, except in cases specified in this law, is prohibited. Creating new income is possible in the form of income-expenditure.
Note - The meaning of income - expense is: In annual budget laws, an amount is projected as income by an institution, and the consumption and expense of that income are allocated to that institution.
C- The Organization is required to design and establish a new revenue-expenditure system for the provinces with the aim of sustainably increasing provincial revenues and improving provincial balances within the framework of efficient and effective incentive mechanisms through the separation of duties and authorities of national and provincial executive bodies and the systematic return of excess revenues to the provinces. The executive regulations of this paragraph shall be prepared by the Organization within three months of the entry into force of this law, in cooperation with the Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance and the Ministry of Interior, and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
Expense credits
Article 18- In order to reduce current costs, improve resource efficiency, and enhance transparency in the spending of executive agencies, the following measures shall be taken:
A- The organization is required to gradually establish a performance-based budgeting system in the executive agencies providing services and products by the end of the second year of the program, in such a way that the forecasting and payment of credits are made based on activities (products and services) in proportion to the cost price and volume of activity.
The executive regulations of this section, including granting authority to executive managers and incentive mechanisms, as well as the criteria and list of executive agencies subject to this decree and related executive regulations, shall be approved by the Council of Ministers upon the proposal of the organization.
b)
1- The salaries, benefits, and remuneration of faculty members and judges are subject to their own employment laws.
2- The salaries, benefits, and receipts of employees of ministries and government institutions, non-governmental public institutions and bodies, and the armed forces are subject to relevant laws.
Note - Increasing the income ceiling upon request of the highest authority in the organization and approval of the Salary and Wage Council is permissible only for sensitive and specific jobs or jobs with specific conditions (and not specific organizations), including in the operational areas of the oil and maritime industries.
C- In all legal cases, granting assistance to the non-governmental sector is permitted in compliance with paragraph "A" of Article (31) of the Law on the Addition of Certain Articles to the Law on the Regulation of Part of Government Financial Regulations (2) approved on 2/4/2014 if it is in line with the missions and duties of the relevant agencies and proportionate to the cost price of the product, goods or services and the assistance program provided. The non-governmental sector will be accountable to the assisting agency for the assistance received.
D- It is prohibited to create and impose any financial burden in excess of the figures stated in the annual budget laws on the executive branch, in various forms of approvals, circulars, instructions, changes in organization, changes in recruitment regulations (in the form of changes in coefficients, legal tables and job classifications and increasing the legal basis), granting permits for any type of recruitment and employment of personnel, guaranteed purchases, compensation for losses, export bonuses, and the like. The responsibility for implementing this ruling lies with the highest official of the executive branch or authorized officials and relevant financial managers.
Note - In order to prevent an increase in budget obligations, any decision-making by executive bodies and decision-making authorities, councils, boards of trustees of universities, and general assemblies of state-owned companies regarding an increase in budget obligations is prohibited without clearly foreseeing the title of the decision and its financial burden in the budget law.
E- The organization is required to include the method and amount of payment of the government's debt for the facilities provided by the government annually in the table of annual budget bills.
C- It is prohibited to create any financial obligation without providing the required funding for pension and insurance funds, municipalities, and other non-governmental public institutions and entities.
Capital Asset Acquisition Plans
Article 19 - In order to organize development projects, reduce their implementation time, and improve the efficiency of resources allocated to this sector, the following measures will be taken:
A.
1- In implementing paragraph (3) of the general policies of the Seventh Five-Year Plan, the government is required to determine the status of capital asset acquisition plans through various means, including public-private partnerships, within the framework of Article (20) of this law and in compliance with other laws and regulations in accordance with the regulations prepared by the organization and approved by the Council of Ministers.
2- Executive agencies should proceed with the assignment of plans to acquire national and provincial capital assets, whether for profit or transfer, or to be shared with the public, private or cooperative sectors, in accordance with the model contracts notified by the organization.
B- Starting construction of projects or sub-projects for the acquisition of national capital assets and increasing the volume of projects licensed under Article (23) of the Law on the Addition of Certain Articles to the Law on the Regulation of Part of Government Financial Regulations (2) without obtaining the permission of the aforementioned article is prohibited and constitutes illegal appropriation of public property.
Also, financing for all capital asset acquisition projects in other budget tables, including the miscellaneous table, is subject to obtaining permission from Article (23) of the Law on the Addition of Certain Articles to the Law on the Regulation of Part of Government Financial Regulations (2) and Transfer to Appendix (1).
Article 20- Executive agencies are required, in cooperation with the organization, to identify new, semi-finished, ready-to-operate, and currently operating capital asset acquisition projects and capital projects that can be partnered with the private and cooperative sectors, and to implement them through a competitive and transparent bidding or auction method, observing the following:
A- The price of the product of the plan (project) in the investment and partnership contract is subject to the financial model of the partnership contract and is excluded from the tariff setting included in all laws and regulations. In case of determining the mandatory price, interfering in the tariff setting or preventing the receipt of the tariff for the price of the product of the plan (project), the difference between the product price calculated based on the financial model and the mandatory price shall be paid from the total funds of the executive body by calculating the relevant damages, otherwise it is considered as an unauthorized seizure of the investor's property.
B- The organization is responsible for the management and responsibility of the public-private partnership. In the case of budgetary commitments of partnership contracts that have already been approved by the organization and the other party has fully fulfilled its commitment, the relevant executive body is obliged to fulfill its commitment to the same extent.
C- The income of the plan (project) in the investment and partnership contract shall enjoy the tax incentives stipulated in parts (1) and (2) of paragraph (e) of Article (132) of the Direct Taxes Law, subject to Article (31) of the Law on Removing Barriers to Competitive Production and Improving the Financial System of the Country, approved on 2/01/2015, and cash contributions to finance the plan (project) of natural and legal persons shall be subject to the exemption of Article (138 bis) of the Additional Direct Taxes Law, approved on 2/01/2015. The plans subject to the “Law on Construction of Development Projects in the Road and Transportation Sector through the Participation of Banks and Other Financial and Monetary Resources of the Country, approved on 1/06/1368, with subsequent amendments and additions” are also subject to this ruling.
D- Issuance of accounts by the Social Security Organization for insurance premiums of employees employed during the exploitation period in partnership contracts is subject to Article (40) of the Law on Removing Barriers to Competitive Production and Improving the Country's Financial System.
E- The relevant executive body may, for the commercialization and granting of incentives for the financial justification of participatory projects, take action to use incentive mechanisms such as granting interest subsidies on facilities and guaranteed purchase of products, pursuant to a regulation prepared by the organization and approved by the Council of Ministers, in compliance with paragraph "T" of Article (18) of this law.
C- Up to ten percent (10%) of the total funds of capital asset acquisition projects or capital projects related to each executive agency, upon request of that agency and approval of the organization, shall be spent on participation in sub-projects (projects) of the same agency and the same chapter in the private, cooperative and non-governmental public sectors.
G- Executive agencies are authorized to enter into long-term exploitation contracts for completed infrastructure, as well as capital asset acquisition plans and capital projects ready for operation and in operation, provided that their use is not changed, in compliance with the general policies of Article 44 (44) of the Constitution.
H- The organization is authorized to use the services of competent consultants to review projects with technical, economic, environmental, and passive defense justifications and to supervise the implementation of the projects.
X- If, upon the proposal of the relevant executive body and with the approval of the organization, philanthropists implement or complete capital asset acquisition projects and spend more than fifty percent (50%) instead of government funds on these projects, they will be entitled to a tax credit of at least twenty-five percent (25%) and at most fifty percent (50%) of the expenses they have made.
In the case of projects where at least fifty percent (50%) of the funds are provided by a charity and the rest is the responsibility of the government, if the charity completes the project with the approval of the institution or organization, the cost incurred is considered one hundred percent (100%) as a tax debt and credit.
The executive regulations of this clause, including the eligible projects, implementation schedule, and the amount of tax credit, shall be approved by the Council of Ministers upon the proposal of the Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance and Organization.
Article 21- The organization is required to review the document of the country's integrated technical and executive system, subject to Article (34) of the Law on Permanent Provisions of National Development Programs, approved on 10/51/1331, within six months of the entry into force of this law, with the approach of final management (control) of the implemented plan based on cost price, quality and implementation time indicators, and submit it to the approval of the Council of Ministers. After the approval of the document of the country's integrated technical and executive system, all institutions that use the country's public funds in any way will be subject to the aforementioned document.
Article 22- The following measures shall be taken with the aim of complying with environmental standards:
A- All new major plans and major development plans implemented by executive agencies, private sectors, cooperatives, and non-governmental public institutions and organizations in the territory, including free trade, industrial, and special economic zones, must be subject to environmental impact assessment by the Environmental Protection Organization before implementation based on environmental indicators, criteria, and standards approved by the Supreme Council for Environmental Protection. The Environmental Protection Organization is required to announce its opinion on the approval or disapproval of the plans, stating the reasons for disapproval, in writing within three months. If three months are not sufficient, the Environmental Protection Organization can extend the deadline by another two months. Failure to announce an opinion within the stipulated deadline shall be deemed approval. The executive regulations of this paragraph, including examples of plans and projects subject to assessment, shall be prepared by the Environmental Protection Organization within three months of the entry into force of this law, and after approval by the Supreme Council for Environmental Protection, shall be submitted to the approval of the Council of Ministers.
Note - If a comment is not made within the specified deadline and this results in environmental damage, the relevant managers are responsible for compensating for the damage.
B- Executive agencies are required to subject their major development plans to a strategic environmental assessment and submit the report to the Environmental Protection Organization for approval. The executive regulations of this clause, including the definition of major development plans, shall be prepared by the Environmental Protection Organization and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
C- The Environmental Protection Organization is authorized to monitor, through trusted and cooperating laboratories, the level of pollution and the self-declaration assessment of polluting units and the calibration of equipment for monitoring pollutants of biological resources. The payment of the tariff for the aforementioned services is the responsibility of the covered units. The executive regulations of this paragraph, including the determination of environmental indicators and criteria and the tariffs for providing services to the covered units, shall be prepared by the Environmental Protection Organization and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
D- Pursuant to paragraph (8) of the general environmental policies and in order to develop the green economy and low-carbon industry and strengthen adaptation and reduce the damages caused by climate change, the Environmental Protection Organization is required to implement the required action plan and legal arrangements in cooperation with the Ministries of Petroleum, Energy, Industry, Mines and Trade, Roads and Urban Development, and Health, Treatment and Medical Education regarding the formulation of the country's climate change management plan during the first year.
E - In order to achieve a favorable environment for the community during the implementation of the program:
1- The Environmental Protection Organization is required to take action, by the end of the second year of the program at the latest, in cooperation with the organization and other relevant executive agencies, to conduct an economic valuation of environmental resources, determine the cost of environmental damage, and how to allocate it for environmental projects based on regulations approved by the Council of Ministers.
2- In order to prevent the spread of human and animal infectious diseases and improve the level of public health in the country's cities and villages, the Ministry of Interior is required to prepare and compile a comprehensive executive plan, including determining the role and duty of each agency in controlling the population of stray animals that transmit diseases to humans, in cooperation with the Ministries of Health, Medical Education and Agricultural Jihad, the Environmental Protection Organization, the Islamic Republic of Iran Broadcasting Organization, municipalities and rural areas, and non-governmental organizations, and with the approach of utilizing the capacity of non-governmental organizations and organizations.
C- The Environmental Protection Organization is required to prepare, within the framework of the laws, short-term and medium-term plans for preventing, adapting to, and combating dust phenomena in the country in the form of a comprehensive plan to combat dust phenomena and an action plan for related executive agencies, and submit them to the Cabinet for approval, and submit a report on the performance of this section to the Agriculture, Water, Natural Resources, and Environment Commission of the Parliament every six months, in order to stabilize dust production centers.
G- In order to protect the environment and public health from the harmful effects of waste and to responsibly manage the resources from which waste is produced:
1- The Environmental Protection Organization is required to prepare, in cooperation with the Ministries of Interior, Industry, Mines and Trade, Power, Oil, Agricultural Jihad, and Health, Treatment and Medical Education, a “National Strategic Waste Management Plan” with the approach of reforming the production and consumption pattern, minimizing waste generation, separation at source, and implementing a circular economy system in the waste management cycle by the end of the first year of the plan, and submit it to the Council of Ministers for approval. The relevant agencies are required to act during the years of implementation of the plan in such a way that the “National Strategic Waste Management Plan” is fully implemented in metropolitan cities and cities in the northern provinces.
2- In order to support units producing materials and energy from waste, large industries such as cement and steel are required to secure part of their energy needs, especially during peak energy consumption months, from solid fuel derived from waste. The Ministry of Energy is also required to guarantee the purchase of electricity produced from waste, the Ministry of Oil is required to guarantee the purchase or issue a license to sell liquid fuels produced from waste, and the Ministry of Agricultural Jihad is required to guarantee the purchase of organic fertilizers resulting from waste recycling processes.
3- The Environmental Protection Organization is required to establish an integrated waste management system with the aim of monitoring and supervising all waste management measures in the country by the end of the first year of the program.
Note - The Environmental Protection Organization is required to prepare the executive regulations of this clause by the end of the first year of the program and submit them to the Council of Ministers for approval, in cooperation with the Ministries of Interior, Industry, Mines and Trade, Power, Petroleum, Agricultural Jihad, and Health, Treatment and Medical Education.
Article 23 - The cost of management services for the acquisition of capital assets of the National Transportation Infrastructure Construction and Development Company, the Islamic Revolution Housing Foundation, the Executive Organization for Governmental and Public Buildings and Facilities, the Iranian Water and Power Resources Development Company, the Specialized Parent Company for the Development and Equipping of National Health Centers and Medical Equipment, and the National Sports Venues Development and Maintenance Company shall be determined up to two and a half percent (2.5%) of the performance of the relevant credit allocation, including the total funds received from the public budget, including cash, treasury bills, and participation bonds, and shall be paid from the credits of the relevant institution.
Obligations and debts
Article 24- In order to regulate the obligations and pay the debts of the government, the following measures shall be taken:
A- Any debt or commitment by executive agencies is subject to the approval of the Organization solely by observing the government debt sustainability index. The ceiling of the outstanding debt of the government and state-owned companies, including the debt to the National Development Fund, during the years of program implementation is a maximum of forty percent (40%) of the gross domestic product, with the government debt share being a maximum of eighteen percentage points of this share. The Government is required to determine the permissible ceiling for issuing letters of guarantee and undertaking issued under its responsibility in the annual budget bills and to submit its report to the Parliament every six months. The Organization is required to include the government’s commitments each year in the ceiling of the annual budget bills and to anticipate the necessary resources for their payment.
Note - The portion of government debt that is created in the form of Islamic financial bonds is included in the debt ceiling calculations with a coefficient of seven tenths (0.7).
B- Acceptance of definitive debts by the government in cases of dispute is subject to special procedures for examining and auditing the claims claimed by individuals from the government and providing the government's commitment ID from the organization.
C- Executive agencies are required to provide the information required by the Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance to assess the sustainability of public sector debt.
D- The Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance is required to convert the outstanding debt to contractors of national and provincial capital asset acquisition projects into securities by the end of the first year of the program, subject to their consent, and to determine a cash flow for them with a specific maturity. These securities, with a maximum maturity of five years, will gradually become tradable in the capital market by the end of the program, based on a plan prepared by the Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance.
The Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance is required to submit a report on the performance of this section to the Planning and Budget, Accounting and Economic Committees of the Parliament every six months.
E- The organization will take legal action to pay the government's legally audited debts to municipalities, the Armed Forces of the Islamic Republic of Iran, the Social Security Organization, and the Khatam al-Anbiya Construction Headquarters until the end of the program. Any new obligations to municipalities and villages that lead to increased costs, and any exemptions and reductions in income without securing its financial resources, are prohibited.
State-owned companies
Article 25- In order to organize and increase the efficiency and effectiveness of state-owned companies and accelerate the transfer of companies that can be transferred, the following measures shall be taken:
A- The government is allowed to revalue the fixed assets of state-owned companies with accumulated losses, subject to Article (4) of the General Accounting Law, and with accumulated losses, whose shares are one hundred percent (100%) owned by the government or state-owned companies, once by the end of the second year of the program. The government's share of the amounts resulting from the revaluation of the aforementioned state-owned companies is exempt from paying taxes and must be deposited, as the case may be, into the capital increase account of the government or the state-owned company that is a shareholder in the aforementioned state-owned companies subject to this clause. The Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance is required to prepare the executive regulations of this clause, including the manner of depreciation of revalued depreciable fixed assets, within three months of the entry into force of this law, and submit them to the approval of the Council of Ministers.
B- State-owned companies are required to submit all investment plans and sub-plans (projects) from their internal resources, subject to Article (87) of the Law on the Regulation of Part of the Government Financial Regulations, approved on 11/27/2001, whose investment amount exceeds sixty times the average transaction quota, to the Economic Council for approval once before commencement.
C- The government is required to take the necessary legal action by the end of the first year of the program, in compliance with Note (72) of the 1973 Budget Law, amended on November 30, 2000, regarding the review of the composition of its stock representation members in the general assemblies of state-owned companies and companies in which the government has management or controlling shares, with the approach of eliminating conflicts of interest.
D- The framework of annual bonuses payable to the CEO, members of the board of directors, members of the executive board, managers of state-owned companies subject to Article (5) of the Civil Service Management Law and companies in which the government has some management or control shares, credit institutions and insurance companies, taking into account the size and complexity of their activities, as well as criteria such as level of education, field of study, experience and management records, and efficiency and productivity, in compliance with the laws, shall be prepared by the Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance in cooperation with the organization and approved by the Council of Ministers. The maximum bonus ceiling is one month of legal salaries and benefits.
Chapter 4 - Tax System Reform
Article 26: In implementing paragraph (4) of the general policies of the Seventh Five-Year Plan and in order to achieve the following quantitative goals, action shall be taken in accordance with the provisions of this chapter:
Table No. (4) - Quantitative objectives of performance indicators for tax system reform
Performance measure
One known
Quantitative goal
At the end of the program
The ratio of tax revenues to GDP is 10%/year.
Tax to spending appropriations ratio 80%/year
The Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance is required to submit a report on the performance indicators of tax system reform to the Parliament annually.
Article 27- In order to increase the share of taxes in the country's general budget;
A- The imposition of any discount, preference, forgiveness, rate reduction, exemption, zero-rate inclusion, and granting of new tax credits, except for cases that, at the discretion of the Parliament, lead to an increase or prosperity in production and exports, is prohibited during the program years. The tax credit referred to in Article (11) of the Knowledge-Based Production Leap Law is not subject to this clause.
Any repeal, amendment, or cancellation of legal provisions in the field of taxation is possible only through relevant laws, subject to this clause.
B- In order to ensure transparency in tax protection, the Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance is required to prepare an annual list of all discounts, tax credits, zero rates, exemptions or remissions, and tax and customs preferences, and calculate the amount of government revenue lost due to the aforementioned items, based on the legal references related to the separation. The organization is also required to publish it in the form of an appendix to the annual budget.
C- The Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance is required, in cooperation with the organization, to draft and submit the necessary legal bills to reduce discounts, tax credits, zero rates, exemptions or remissions, and tax and customs preferences in order to discourage unproductive activities, organize unnecessary exemptions, and strengthen exemptions that lead to production growth within six months of the entry into force of this law.
D- In implementing paragraph (4) of the general policies of the Seventh Five-Year Plan based on the prosperity of production and tax justice, the Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance is required, in cooperation with the Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare, to provide legal arrangements by the end of the first year of the plan to abstract tax litigation processes from the National Tax Affairs Organization and insurance litigation from the Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare, and to establish independent tax and insurance litigation centers.
E- The Central Bank, all credit institutions, Qarz al-Hasaneh funds and municipalities, the Traffic Police of the Islamic Republic of Iran Police Command (Rahor Faraja), and the National Real Estate and Documents Registration Organization are required to provide the information requested by the National Tax Affairs Organization in the implementation of tax laws online. In case of violation of this ruling, the aforementioned authorities will be subject to the deprivation of Article (202) of the Amended Direct Taxes Law of 1394/4/31. Illegal use of the aforementioned information is considered a crime and the violator will be sentenced to the sixth degree of Ta’zir punishment under Article (19) of the Islamic Penal Code.
C- The exemption of Clause "B" of Article (159) of the Law of the Fifth Five-Year Development Plan of the Islamic Republic of Iran is valid only for the production and mining activities of industrial and mining units whose exploitation license or extraction contract was issued during the implementation period of the aforementioned law.
G- During the program years, the rial figures subject to Articles (44), (46) and (47) of the Direct Taxes Law and their notes will be adjusted and applied based on the consumer price index.
Chapter 5 - Pension Fund Reform (Management, Financial, and Metric Reforms)
Article 28 - In order to reduce the financial imbalance of pension organizations and funds, prevent financial instability, and also reduce their dependence on the public budget, and improve the quality and reform the structure of social insurance, from the first year of the program's implementation, the following measures will be taken in the national, military, social security, and other pension funds affiliated with executive agencies and non-governmental public institutions and bodies:
A- The government is required to pay its audited debt (in accordance with clause "e" of Article (7) of the Law on the Structure of the Comprehensive Welfare and Social Security System, approved on 21/02/2004) to the Social Security Organization and the Social Insurance Fund for Farmers, Villagers and Nomads during the implementation of the program in the form of annual budgets. All payments and contributions from the government to pension funds, in excess of the employer's share and the government's share, as well as all unpaid legal guarantees, are considered as payment of the government's debt.
The Steel Pension Fund is also subject to this provision in the event of a legal claim from the government. Any government assistance in the form of an annual budget in excess of debts is also considered a government claim. Creating any new obligations for the Social Security Organization and the Social Insurance Fund for Farmers, Villagers, and Nomads without providing resources during the implementation of the program is prohibited. The debt subject to this clause must have been approved by the National Audit Office after deducting government assistance in the annual budget laws.
B- During the implementation of the program in the form of an annual budget, the government is required to pay its audited debt to the Social Security Organization through cash payments in the annual budget and legal securities, and the transfer of shares, properties, and assets in excess of the government's needs within the framework of the laws, as well as through clearing methods, the transfer of shares of profitable listed and unlisted companies in compliance with the general policies of Article 44 (44), the transfer of gas and oil condensates, feed and energy of production units belonging to the Social Security Organization and its subsidiaries, the transfer of Islamic securities (common in the money and capital markets) issued by the government, the granting of government guarantees and agreed-upon concessions, and the transfer of economically justified projects with a high percentage of progress, and other transferable items in compliance with Article 53 (53) of the Constitution.
C- The Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare is required, in cooperation with the organization, to prepare "Investment Regulations for Organizations and Pension Funds" within six months of the effective date of this law, in order to enhance the funds' reserves, protect the intergenerational rights and obligations of the insured, strengthen corporate governance, transparency in investment affairs, profitability and efficiency of the investment portfolio, reduce entrepreneurship, change the approach towards stock market investments, accountability of the board of directors and principles of risk analysis, in addition to the regulations contained in paragraph "e" of Article (15) of the Law on the Structure of the Comprehensive Welfare and Social Security System, and submit it to the approval of the Council of Ministers.
D- Pension funds, including national and military, and social security funds, are required to transfer all shares owned by them and their subsidiaries and affiliated companies, in which the pension funds' and subsidiaries' shares are more than twenty percent (20%) and whose value is less than three hundred times the average transaction quota (subject of the Tenders Law) within the first two years of the program at the latest.
The government is required to prepare a transfer schedule within three months of the entry into force of this law, submit it to the Council of Ministers for approval, and submit its report to the parliament. It is also required to submit a report on transfers to the parliament every six months. The Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare is required to organize legal arrangements in such a way that transfers are carried out completely, correctly and legally, to the extent determined by the government each year.
E- The Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance, in cooperation with the Organization, the State Administrative and Employment Organization, the Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare, and the Ministry of Defense and Armed Forces Support, is required to prepare, within three months of the entry into force of this law, instructions on how to qualify the managing directors and members of the boards of directors of subsidiary and affiliated companies of pension funds, including civil and military, and social security, as well as individuals who are introduced as members of the boards of directors/executive boards on behalf of shareholders in the aforementioned companies, and submit them to the Council of Ministers for approval.
Any appointment to the positions subject to this clause from the date of notification of the aforementioned directive will be based on its mechanism. The funds subject to this order are required to adapt the current incumbents of the positions subject to this order to the general and specific conditions foreseen in the aforementioned directive within six months from the date of notification of the directive and to take steps to replace those who do not meet the desired conditions.
The responsibility for implementing this ruling will lie with the members of the general assembly of the companies involved, and violators of its implementation will be sentenced to dismissal from government and public services for two years. Other shareholders present at the general assembly, other than representatives of the pension funds subject to this clause and representatives of all their subsidiaries and affiliated institutions and companies, will be exempt from the scope of this ruling.
The Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance is required to submit a report on the performance of clauses "p", "t", and "d" of this article to the economic and social committees of the Parliament every six months.
C- Employers subject to paragraph (4) of Article (2) of the Social Security Law, whether natural or non-governmental legal entities, provided that they are not covered by pension insurance in other funds in accordance with the procedure stipulated in Article (28) of the aforementioned law, can be included in the scope of the Social Security Law. The executive regulations subject to this paragraph, including the beneficiaries, the executive process, the definition of continuity of insurance coverage, and the wage on which the insurance premium is deducted, shall be prepared by the Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare in cooperation with the Ministry of Industry, Mines and Trade and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
G- Freight and passenger transportation service providers who operate through virtual platforms and do not have pension insurance are allowed to insure themselves with the Social Security Organization. The executive regulations on the subject of this paragraph shall be prepared upon the proposal of the Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
H- The exemption of the employer's contribution from paying the retirement deduction for persons whose years of insurance exceed thirty years from the date of implementation of this law shall be repealed in general and specific laws and regulations.
X- In order to ensure the sustainability of insurance and pension funds and reduce their dependence on the public budget, organize insurance exemptions and organize the insurance coverage groups subject to government assistance, complete insurance exemptions for insured persons without an employer in the Social Security Organization, including those subject to the Social Insurance Law for Carpet Weavers, Carpet Weavers, and Handicraft Workers with Identification (Code) approved in 1381/8/58 and individuals subject to Clause "Z" of Note (14) of the 1386 National Budget Law and Clause "B" of Article (7) of the Law on Targeting Subsidies approved in 1381/80/15 with subsequent amendments and additions, are subject to the assessment of the capacity test by the Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor, and Social Welfare and being in the first four income deciles. In the case of insured persons who are in the fifth deciles and beyond during the years of program implementation, half a percent of the existing insurance exemption will be deducted annually for each decile increase.
The executive regulations of this clause shall be prepared by the Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare in cooperation with the organization and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
D- The twenty percent (20%) exemption from the employer's contribution, subject to the Law on Exemption from Payment of Insurance Contributions for Employers with a Maximum of Five Workers, approved in 1361/11/26, with subsequent amendments and additions, for employers whose annual income is more than fifteen times the exemption subject to Article (84) of the Direct Taxes Law, will be reduced by half a percentage point annually during the implementation of the program.
The implementing regulations of this clause for the workshops covered by this clause shall be prepared by the Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers. The government's contribution to the employer's share in paying the aforementioned insurance premium shall be equal to the minimum wage and any excess thereof shall be fully borne by the employer.
The period of general service of the insured persons of the Social Security Organization, subject to Note (1) of Article (14) of the Labor Law approved on 2/7/1368, as well as subscribers of other funds, upon request of the insured person, based on a legal ruling, the time of deposit in the case of employees and the last salary, the basis for payment of insurance premiums in the case of those subject to the Labor Law or the average of the aforementioned amounts, as the case may be, during one year prior to the time of application, whichever is greater, is calculated in their insurance records. The basis for payment of insurance premiums is equal to the percentages determined in each fund, minus the percentage of insurance premiums related to treatment. The government's contribution to the employer's share in paying the aforementioned insurance premiums is equal to the minimum wage, in accordance with existing laws and regulations, and the excess is fully borne by the insured person.
R
1- In order to establish justice in the payment of salaries of employees and retirees, as well as to align the salaries of retirees with ninety percent (90%) of the salaries and allowances subject to deductions of similar and equivalent employees, the government is obliged to implement the necessary action plan by the end of the third year. This increase from 1403 will be forty percent (40%) in the first year and thirty percent (30%) in the second and third years each of the difference up to ninety percent (90%). The executive regulations of this part will be approved by the Council of Ministers.
2- In line with the implementation of Article (96) of the Social Security Law approved on 1354/4/30 with subsequent amendments and additions, the Social Security Organization is required to take steps during the first three years of the program to adjust the pensions of non-minimum earners in such a way that at the end of the third year of the program, the ratio of the retiree's pension to the minimum wage of the same year is proportional to ninety percent (90%) of the ratio of the first retirement pension to the minimum wage of the year the pension is established.
This adjustment will be forty percent (40%) in the first year and thirty percent (30%) in the second and third years each, up to the aforementioned ninety percent (90%).
This ruling will not negate the rights of minimum wage earners in accordance with relevant laws, including Article (111) of the Social Security Law.
3- The Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare is required to take legal action by the end of the second year of the program to adjust the pension payments of the Social Insurance Fund for Farmers, Villagers and Nomads based on insurance calculations and within the framework of paragraphs (3) and (4) of the general social security policies, in proportion to the credit received in the annual budgets.
G- Establishing pensions for all pension fund insured persons (including national, military, social security and other pension funds of institutions, institutions and banks) is based on the average of the last two years of service leading to the received retirement, which has a retirement deduction by applying the salary coefficient of the retirement year.
Note 1- The following shall apply in the event of additional benefits from this article:
1- Retirees who are subject to their own laws.
2- Retirees who are subject to the provisions of paragraph "b" of Article (18) of this law.
3- Veterans who are subject to their own laws and regulations.
Note 2: Exemption from paying the deductible for insured persons after thirty years of service does not prevent the full application of the pension based on the income received during the last two years of service leading to retirement with the aforementioned coefficient in the last year of service.
Article 29 - In order to reduce the imbalance of pension funds and strengthen the ability of the funds to carry out the assigned tasks from the beginning of the first year of the program's implementation:
1- Insurers who have more than 28 years of insurance history will not have their mandatory years of insurance added to their retirement years.
2- For insured persons who have a total insurance history of 25 to 28 years, two months will be added to their mandatory insurance years for retirement for each year until retirement.
3- For those insured with 20 to 25 years of insurance history, a quarterly amount will be added to their mandatory years of insurance for retirement for each year until retirement.
4- Insurers who have a total insurance history of 15 to 20 years will have four months added to their mandatory insurance years for retirement for each year until retirement.
5- Insurers who have less than 15 years of insurance history in accordance with the laws will have five years added to their mandatory insurance years for retirement.
Note 1- The implementation of all or part of the above-mentioned provisions is conditional on the insured's age at the time of retirement not exceeding 62 years for men and 55 years for women. In any case, the maximum mandatory years of insurance for retirement will be 35 years for men and 30 years for women.
Note 2 - The above amendments to the laws related to pension funds will be permanent, with the exception of funds whose minimum mandatory years of insurance for the retirement of their insured persons are greater than the figures mentioned in Note (1).
Note 3: Veterans, the disabled, and those employed in difficult and harmful occupations are subject to their own specific laws.
Note 4: The persons subject to this ruling, with their own consent and the approval of the relevant agencies, may continue to serve in addition to the periods mentioned in parts (2) to (5) of this clause until the age limit stipulated in the relevant laws, as the case may be.
Note 5 - If the agencies do not need the services of some employees, they may, on a case-by-case basis, issue retirement orders for them without considering the periods mentioned in sections (2) to (5), upon the proposal of the highest official in the agency and the approval of the First Vice President, based on relevant laws.
Note 6 - Individuals who, upon their own request, wish to retire without observing the aforementioned deadline, may retire in accordance with the relevant laws and without observing sections (2) to (5), and their pension rights will be established in proportion to the years of service stated in the aforementioned sections (in proportion to their years of insurance coverage to the mandatory years of insurance coverage for their retirement).
The implementing regulations for this article will be prepared by the Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare within six months and will be approved by the Council of Ministers.
Chapter 6 - Social Security, Supportive Policies, and Fair Income Distribution
Article 30: In implementing paragraphs (1) and (5) of the general policies of the Seventh Five-Year Plan and in order to achieve the following quantitative goals, action shall be taken in accordance with the provisions of this chapter:

The ratio of the tenth decile to the first decile in the rural sector is 9.3.
The ratio of the tenth decile to the first decile in the urban sector is 10.3.
Absolute poverty percentage 0
The organization is required to submit a report on the performance indicators of this article to the parliament annually.
Article 31- In order to develop economic justice and improve income distribution, the following measures will be taken by the end of the first year of the program:
A- The Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare is authorized, within the relevant resources ceiling in the annual budget laws, to design and establish a multi-layered social security system based on means testing with the aim of reducing absolute poverty and improving income distribution, and by identifying low-income groups up to the seventh income decile with a community-based approach, to provide essential items in the form of a basic livelihood package to low-income households in the form of electronic vouchers in addition to legal subsidies.
B- The Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare is required to fully launch the single window for support services and the electronic welfare file of individuals or households, in accordance with Subsection (3) of Clause “A” of Article One of the Law on Certain Provisions Related to Reforming the Structure of the National Budget, approved on 1/4/1400. Executive agencies that support vulnerable groups in any way are required to provide all their cash and non-cash support through this window. Applicants for support must also apply through this window to receive the aforementioned support.
The Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare is required to submit a report on the performance of this section to the Social Commission and the Deputy for Oversight of the Parliament every six months.
C- The Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare is required, within the framework of general social security policies, to take action through public companies to create a time bank to provide free services to people who need special care, including care for the elderly and disabled, so that after attracting people interested in providing services, they or people introduced by them will be supported in proportion to the amount and type of services provided when they need them.
T-
1- Considering the dignity and status of the families of martyrs and veterans and the necessity of expanding services to them, the government is obliged to take the necessary legal action through relevant authorities and with the aim of strengthening justice and targeted support, promoting effectiveness and increasing the satisfaction of the target community in providing services, to amend and consolidate all existing laws and regulations in the field of providing services to veterans, including the Comprehensive Law on Providing Services to Veterans approved on 1386/04/3, the Law on the Status of Employment of Martyrs, Disabled Veterans and Missing Persons of the Islamic Revolution and the Imposed War approved on 1376/02/30, and the Law on Employment and Social Facilities for Veterans of the Islamic Revolution approved on 1374/03/31 by the end of the first year of the program, in compliance with legal arrangements.
2- Articles (86) to (91) of the Law on the Sixth Five-Year Plan for the Economic, Social and Cultural Development of the Islamic Republic of Iran, approved on 24/51/1391, shall be implemented with the following provisions in mind:
1-2- The ruling regarding the net ceiling for continuous and non-continuous salaries and benefits and other payments from any location and under any title, including pension insurance exemption and tax exemption subject to Articles (37) and (56) of the "Comprehensive Service Provision to Veterans" Law, does not apply to veterans.
2.2- The benefits and privileges of the veterans' laws will be extended to veterans and martyrs defending the Holy Shrine, as well as veterans and martyrs of security, during the implementation of the program.
E- During the implementation of the program, in addition to paying the current subsidy, the government is required to provide and pay the minimum pension to the families of beneficiaries supported by the Imam Khomeini Relief Committee (RA) and the National Welfare Organization every year, proportional to the level of deprivation, based on an average of twenty percent (20%) of the minimum wage approved by the Supreme Labor Council, within the framework of the annual budget and from the revenue of the law on targeting subsidies by eliminating high-income households and in the form of an independent tier through the aforementioned agencies.
Note - The Imam Khomeini Relief Committee (RA) will take action regarding this clause in accordance with its statute.
C- The Imam Khomeini Relief Committee (RA) and the National Welfare Organization are required to provide stable jobs to the people under their coverage and also to the low-income people of the society in small and home employment projects with the approach of production chains and determining the share in the growth of national production, with the aim of empowering and creating sustainable income. The government is required to foresee the required resources including bank Qarz-ul-Hasanah facilities, donations from philanthropists, public institutions and headquarters and foundations of the Islamic Revolution, taking into account the acceptable per capita employment in the annual budget.
Chapter 7 - Food security and improving agricultural production

Article 33: In order to increase the self-sufficiency rate and the optimal and integrated exploitation of resources and factors of production, especially water and soil resources, as well as to improve the livelihoods of farmers, villagers, and nomads, the Ministry of Agricultural Jihad is required to take action on the following matters, in cooperation with the organization and other relevant executive bodies, based on land planning documents and climatic conditions, commensurate with regional talents and capabilities, and economic advantages, and in compliance with environmental considerations and the livelihoods of the beneficiaries, in compliance with the general policies of the system, including the general policies of the environment and natural resources:
A- Prepare an optimal production plan (cultivation pattern) for the products subject to Article (31) of the Law on Increasing Productivity in the Agricultural and Natural Resources Sector, approved on 1389/04/23, based on a five-year plan, and determine it every year up to three months before the start of the agricultural year in each watershed and plain, and implement all its price and non-price supports based on this plan.
The optimal production plan (cultivation pattern) is determined based on climatic, water and soil conditions, restrictions on the cultivation of non-strategic crops in lands suitable for strategic crops, intensive cultivation of strategic crops in fertile and suitable plains, comparative advantages, added value, economic and climatic conditions, and its optimal limit in the country.
B- Support for farmers is provided in proportion to the degree of compliance with the determined optimal production plan (cultivation pattern). Otherwise, any support related to the said plan is tantamount to illegal seizure of public property.
Note - In order to compensate for the imposed cost resulting from government interventions in the market through mandatory pricing, the government is required to pay the difference between the mandatory price and the market price determined by the Ministry of Agricultural Jihad within the ceiling of resources foreseen in the annual budget.
C- By the final year of implementation of this law, take legal action regarding the gradual transfer of price and non-price, technical, financial, and facility support for the agricultural and food production sector to the end of the production chain (producer) based on the quality and quantity of the product produced and in accordance with the optimal production plan (cultivation pattern).
The Ministry of Agricultural Jihad is required to submit an annual report on the performance of clauses "A", "B", and "C" of this article to the Parliament.
D - For the production of basic products:
1- The Ministry of Agricultural Jihad shall take legal action within a maximum of six months from the entry into force of this law regarding the production and export of large-scale greenhouse products in the form of agricultural towns and agricultural hubs in accordance with the legal criteria and regulations governing them and the relevant areas.
2- Take action to complete and implement agricultural development projects, especially in the areas of water and soil, including the implementation of the second step (phase) of the agricultural land restoration and improvement plan (550,000 hectares in Khuzestan and Ilam), the comprehensive plan for the construction and organization of agricultural water and soil resource infrastructure in the northern provinces at the level of one million hectares, and the completion, development, and exploitation of tropical and cold-weather projects in coordination with the Ministry of Energy in the form of an annual budget and in accordance with the amount of resources allocated.
3- Take action regarding the exploitation of the advanced smart agricultural system of subsurface irrigation (Peeshran Institute Project), based on moisture supply, soil nutrition and subsurface aeration in Karun agricultural and industrial lands and agricultural lands over ten hectares in the entire country, in the form of an annual budget and the amount of resources allocated, in such a way that in the aforementioned lands, agricultural water consumption is gradually reduced by at least fifty percent (50%), directly or through other sectors, including private, cooperative and non-governmental sectors, and production productivity is improved by at least one and a half times, and the launch of animal feed (alfalfa silage) production lines is carried out in such a way that dependence on animal feed imports is reduced.
4- The water consumption tariff for greenhouse crops in agricultural areas and towns, nurseries and seed and seedling production stations, and forest parks of the Natural Resources and Watershed Management Organization of the country is calculated at the approved rate for agricultural activities, regardless of any source of supply, and agricultural complexes and towns benefit from the benefits stated in Article (81) of the Law on the Addition of Certain Articles to the Law on the Regulation of Part of Government Financial Regulations (2).
5- Take steps to save one percent (1%) of agricultural groundwater consumption annually through the cultivation of drought and salinity-resistant varieties and the development of salinity management methods in the country's vulnerable coastal areas.
6- The Natural Resources and Watershed Management Organization of the country is authorized to utilize the capacity of implementers, operators, indigenous and local people, villagers, and other qualified individuals in the form of cooperative companies for watershed management and forestry operations in the form of a technical and executive system and formal contracts without creating an employment relationship, in compliance with laws and regulations.
E- To downsize and increase the effectiveness of the agricultural education, research, and technology system, redefine the role of the government, and increase the role of the non-governmental sector, redesign the organizational structure, duties, and powers of the Agricultural Research, Education, and Extension Organization (ARO) and the research and development institutions of the Ministry of Agricultural Jihad to perform the functions of creative management, development, and dissemination of technology and innovation, in compliance with the laws, regulations, and general policies of the system, including general policies on the environment and natural resources, and submit the plan to the Supreme Administrative Council for approval by the end of the first year.
C- To increase the productivity of non-governmental funds supporting the development of the agricultural sector, in compliance with the relevant rules and regulations, take steps to merge, reform the structure, and reduce the number and diversity of non-governmental funds supporting the development of the agricultural sector, subject to Article (17) of the Law on Increasing the Productivity of the Agricultural Sector and Natural Resources.
G- The government is authorized to provide the necessary credit in annual budget bills to increase the cash capital of the Agricultural Bank with the aim of increasing the capital adequacy ratio of the Agricultural Bank to at least eight percent (8%). In the event of an increase in the government’s capital in the Agricultural Bank, the Bank is required to pay at least five times the increase in capital to the agricultural sector as facilities. The Ministries of Economic Affairs and Finance and Agricultural Jihad are required to submit an annual report on the performance of this clause to the Parliament.
H
1- In order to allocate technical and credit assistance to production cooperatives and establish weekly markets and direct supply stations for agricultural products (with the aim of reducing the price of goods), municipalities are required, upon request from the Ministry of Agricultural Jihad, to provide suitable spaces at expert prices to rural and nomadic producers to carry out the above activities.
2- The Central Insurance of the Islamic Republic of Iran is obliged, in cooperation with the Ministry of Agricultural Jihad and the Presidential Vice-President for Science, Technology and Knowledge-Based Economy, to take appropriate measures to facilitate the entry of commercial insurance into the civil liability insurance process of companies and institutions providing technical and engineering services in the field of agricultural technology and knowledge-based companies and institutions.
3- The Agricultural Insurance Fund is required to provide compulsory all-risk insurance for basic products (wheat, barley, rice, legumes, red and white meat, sugar, corn, and oilseeds) against losses caused by natural disasters and accidents through the brokerage of insurance companies. The farmer's share insurance premium is paid from the farmer's claims and from the guaranteed purchase line credit.
4- The Ministry of Agricultural Jihad is required to take action, in compliance with Article (7) of the National Data and Information Management Law, to establish an integrated spatial, descriptive, and market information system and create an appropriate structure for sharing various data, in connection with the comprehensive Iranian trade system, by the end of the first year of the program.
Article 34- In order to increase the level of health and safety of food and prevent conflicts of interest, the Ministries of Health, Treatment and Medical Education and Agricultural Jihad are authorized to issue licenses to establish centers of technical and health officials in compliance with the Law on Facilitating the Issuance of Business Licenses, in order to streamline the government's health and technical supervision over factories and workshops for the production of food, beverages, cosmetics and hygiene products, subject to the Law on Food, Beverages and Cosmetics, approved on 22/04/1346, with subsequent amendments and additions, and the Law on Regulations on Medical and Pharmaceutical Affairs and Food and Beverage Products, approved on 29/03/1334, with subsequent amendments and additions, and slaughterhouses and factories for the production and preparation of raw animal products, subject to the Law on the National Veterinary Organization, approved on 24/03/1350, with subsequent amendments and additions, and the Law on Sharia Supervision of Slaughter and Hunting, approved on 24/11/1387.
The executive regulations of this article shall be prepared within three months of the entry into force of this law upon the joint proposal of the aforementioned ministries and in cooperation with the Ministry of Justice and the Legal Affairs Office of the President, and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
Article 35–
A- The certification of agricultural products in order to create the ability to track and identify the origin of manufactured products and optimize the consumption of inputs at the origin is carried out by the Ministry of Agricultural Jihad in partnership with the Iranian Chamber of Agricultural and Natural Resources Guilds and the Agricultural Engineering and Natural Resources Organization of the Islamic Republic of Iran.
for-
1- The release and cultivation of any genetically modified crop produced domestically or abroad is prohibited on the country's lands.
2- Conducting laboratory and greenhouse research and studies on transgenic products in universities, research institutes and centers, and knowledge-based companies is permitted in compliance with the Biosafety Law of the Islamic Republic of Iran, approved on 7/5/1388.
3- The Ministry of Health, Treatment and Medical Education is obliged to supervise the production and supply of food products that use genetically modified products in their production within the framework of domestic laws and regulations, in line with general health-oriented policies and in coordination with other relevant agencies. All importers and producers of food and beverage products that use genetically modified raw materials are obliged to place labels on these products. In the event of failure to label, the Ministry of Health, Treatment and Medical Education is obliged to suspend the health licenses of the violating units and refer the violators to legal authorities.
4- The Ministry of Agricultural Jihad is required to reduce the import of oil, oilseeds, livestock inputs, and transgenic agricultural products by at least fifty percent (50%) by the end of the program by increasing productivity, promoting the cultivation of low-water-consuming forage and oil crops that are appropriate to the country's climate, reforming and improving forage storage methods, improving the quality of livestock and poultry feed, and importing non-genetically modified products. The Ministry of Agricultural Jihad is also authorized to reduce the raw sale of livestock, poultry, and aquatic inputs by fifty percent (50%) by the end of the program in order to reduce the country's dependence on livestock inputs and utilize the capacity of livestock feed factories. Poultry, livestock, and aquaculture units can produce ready-made feed in their production units after obtaining legal permits from the Ministry of Agricultural Jihad.
The Ministry of Agricultural Jihad is required to submit a report on the performance of this article to the Parliament's Agriculture, Water, Natural Resources, and Environment Committee every six months.
Article 36 – The National Natural Resources and Watershed Management Organization is responsible for preserving, restoring, and developing forests within the framework of the sustainable forest management plan and modern forestry. Any exploitation of timber from the forest and harvesting of forest trees is prohibited.
Note 1- Harvesting of uprooted, broken, and fallen trees resulting from natural factors (storms, floods, heavy snow, landslides, and extensive drifts) and pest-infested trees that cannot be restored (outside the management of municipalities), as well as hazardous trees on the edges of forest roads and forest parks, is carried out solely by the Natural Resources and Watershed Management Organization of the country with the approval of the head of the said organization.
Note 2 - The Natural Resources and Watershed Management Organization of the country is required to implement timber cultivation projects in suitable lands and forest areas lacking cover and degraded (on an economic scale), as well as the exploitation of annual plantations and forests for the purpose of timber cultivation based on the approved plan through private sector investment, through a call for proposals and determination of the winner by concluding periodic and long-term economic contracts (without transfer of ownership).
