Water management system
Article 38 – In order to improve the decision-making system, establish desirable governance of the country’s water resources, create a unified approach in carrying out affairs related to the implementation of policies and the integrated management of water resources and uses at the national level and in watersheds, with priority given to controlling border waters and basins and sub-basins encompassing the four regions under the management of the Environmental Protection and Wetlands Organization, the following measures shall be taken:
A- The Ministry of Energy is required to prepare a plan to reform the structure and statutes of its subsidiary companies through merger or dissolution by the end of the second year of the program, with the aim of managing the water sector based on the country's watershed boundaries and a fair water distribution system, reducing parallel structures and overhead costs, separating governance and management duties, and eliminating any conflict of corporate interests. After approval by the country's administrative and employment organization, it will submit it to the Council of Ministers for approval.
B- In order to ensure the sustainability of the land and the integrated management of the country's wetlands and lakes, the government (Ministry of Energy) is required to establish the necessary executive mechanisms by the end of the first year of the program to implement the National Action Plan for Wetlands Protection and Management, with priority given to implementing comprehensive ecosystem management programs, allocating and meeting environmental water needs, and preventing unauthorized harvesting of these rights, emphasizing the duties and authorities of the Ministries of Agricultural Jihad, Energy and Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts, and the Environmental Protection Organization, and, as far as possible, by attracting the participation of users and local communities in the plains surrounding the wetlands and lakes.
C- During the years of implementation of this law, in order to strengthen and preserve the country's water resources, the Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance (Customs of the Islamic Republic of Iran) is required to collect annually half a percent (0.5%) of the value of agricultural and food products with high water content exported contrary to the cultivation pattern as duties and add half a percent (0.5%) to these duties every year until the amount reaches two and a half percent (2.5%) at the end of the fifth year and deposit the income from the above duties into the relevant income line with the National Treasury. Seventy percent (70%) of the income from the implementation of this clause shall be provided to the Ministry of Agricultural Jihad for the purpose of restoring canals, increasing water and agricultural product productivity, implementing watershed management plans and cultivation patterns, and the remaining thirty percent (30%) shall be provided to the Ministry of Energy for the purpose of installing smart meters for agricultural water wells. The list of agricultural and food products subject to this clause shall be prepared, approved and notified annually by the Minister of Agricultural Jihad at the beginning of each year.
The Ministries of Agricultural Jihad and Economic Affairs and Finance are required to submit an annual performance report on this section to the Parliament.
D- The Ministry of Energy is required to establish a market for the exchange of unconventional waters in the first year of implementation of this law, taking into account the issues related to the water resources balance sheet and in order to balance the groundwater tables, while preserving water use and preventing pollution and soil degradation. In order to encourage investors, it is required to provide the necessary support through granting licenses in accordance with the Law on Facilitating the Issuance of Business Licenses approved on 24/12/1400 with subsequent amendments and additions, technical and credit assistance, and the use of banking facilities. The executive regulations of this clause, including the mechanism of this market, the conditions of exchange, the volume, period, and type of water consumption, shall be prepared with the proposal of the Ministry of Energy and in cooperation with the organization, the Environmental Protection Organization, and the Ministries of Economic Affairs and Finance, Agricultural Jihad and Industry, Mines and Trade, and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
E- Cash and non-cash expenses incurred by real and legal donors in the construction, development, and completion of water supply projects and the implementation of watershed and aquifer management operations and the restoration and development of natural resources within the framework of approved national and provincial plans with the approval of the Ministry of Energy and the Ministry of Agricultural Jihad (the country's Natural Resources and Watershed Management Organization) are considered acceptable tax expenses.
C- The Ministry of Energy is required, in cooperation with relevant agencies, to prepare a comprehensive flood prevention and monitoring (control) plan for the country, with priority given to high-risk watersheds and taking into account the duties of relevant agencies, within two years, and submit it to the organization and the country's crisis management organization for implementation and provision of credit resources.
Note 1- The Ministry of Energy is required to announce the location of bottlenecks (intersection structures lacking the necessary drainage to pass through floods) to the Ministries of Interior and Roads and Urban Development, respectively for urban and suburban intersection structures, within one month of the entry into force of this law, in order to remove blockages, improve and correct the technical and geometric conditions of the aforementioned structures. The Ministries of Interior and Roads and Urban Development are required to prioritize the aforementioned structures based on high risk, prepare, approve and announce an operational plan within six months to remove blockages, improve and correct the technical and geometric conditions of these structures, and implement the approved plan within two years. Municipalities are required to implement the plans from their internal resources based on the announcement of the Ministry of Interior’s plan.
Note 2 - Watershed and aquifer management activities aimed at preventing and controlling floods from their source in upstream watersheds by the National Natural Resources and Watershed Management Organization are among the measures of the country's comprehensive flood prevention and monitoring (control) plan.
Note 3- In order to improve the practical and applied protection of rivers and flood management in the country, a comprehensive management approach to watersheds using institutional coherence and public participation is mandatory. Study, planning, implementation and monitoring of measures to protect rivers and other surface water courses and flood management are carried out based on basin planning.
f-
1- The Ministries of Power and Agricultural Jihad are required to review all of their ongoing projects, taking into account complementary projects, including main and secondary irrigation and drainage networks, with the aim of achieving positive balance and increasing productivity, and to take action to amend the objectives and operations of the aforementioned projects and sub-projects with the aim of making them justifiable by the end of the first year of implementation of this law.
Deepwater projects in Sistan and Baluchestan Province are not subject to the revision of this section and remain in force.
2- Legal measures should be taken to control common and border waters, dredging the Arvand River, transferring fresh water from the Sea of 
Oman to the eastern regions, developing technology and drilling operations, and exploiting deep waters, especially in the province of Sistan and Baluchestan, with the participation of the non-governmental sector, and increasing the rights of the Hirmand River.
H- The Ministry of Energy is obliged to take the necessary measures in cooperation with the Ministries of Jihad and Agriculture and the Ministry of the Interior, and by utilizing public participation, the government's share of which is included in the annual budget from the pre-sale of extracted water, to increase the volume of extracted water in the country by at least fifteen percent (15%) of the long-term average annual precipitation (five percent (5%) from the management (control) of surface waters, five percent (5%) through watershed management and aquifer management, and five percent (5%) through the extraction of atmospheric waters and rainwater extraction systems and the reduction of evaporation from water storage, transmission, and distribution systems). The amendment or revision of Table No. (7) of the law (subject of Article (37) of this law), proportionate to the water extracted from the operation of this clause, shall be approved by the Parliament.
The Ministry of Energy is required to submit a report on the performance of this article to the Parliament every six months.
Water consumption and efficiency management
Article 39 – In order to improve the optimal water consumption pattern and improve productivity, the following measures shall be taken:
A- The Ministry of Energy is required to amend the tariff for household subscribers in the country in such a way that, taking into account the geographical regions of the country, the tariff for household subscribers covered by the Imam Khomeini Relief Committee (RA) and the National Welfare Organization up to the consumption pattern ceiling is set at zero, subscribers up to the consumption pattern ceiling are set as subsidies, and high-consumption subscribers (above the consumption pattern) are set as non-subsidized and based on the step-up model (EBT). The water consumption pattern of the aforementioned households is calculated based on per capita consumption and based on Note (4) of Article (1) of the Law on the Development and Optimization of Urban and Rural Drinking Water in the Country, approved on 12/24/1394.
1- The branch fee and water charges for commercial and administrative uses shall be calculated, as the case may be, in accordance with the executive regulations approved by the Council of Ministers.
2- Exemption or discount in tariffs for uses that are subject to exemption or discount according to the laws are determined solely within the ceiling of the consumption pattern or contractual capacity or exploitation and usage license, and the calculation of the tariff in excess of the aforementioned consumption is carried out based on the applicable laws.
3- Water and wastewater service providers are required to provide and install measuring instruments with a valid standard for new urban and rural subscribers. The companies are allowed to replace these instruments for existing subscribers (with priority for high-consumption). The cost of installing and providing smart instruments for high-consumption urban and rural subscribers (above the consumption pattern) is the responsibility of the subscribers or operators, and payment in installments is permitted.
Financial resources for the costs of installing and providing smart metering devices for urban and rural subscribers are included in the annual budget at the level of the consumption pattern and below.
The Ministry of Energy is required to submit a report on the performance of this section to the Parliament every six months.
Note 1- The Ministries of Oil and Energy are required to amend the water, electricity, and gas tariffs of households covered by the Imam Khomeini Relief Committee (RA) and the National Welfare Organization in such a way that, taking into account geographical regions, the consumption pattern ceiling (in proportion to per capita consumption for water tariffs) is set at zero. The aforementioned appropriations are foreseen in annual budget bills.
Note 2- Individuals covered by the Imam Khomeini Relief Committee (RA) and the National Welfare Organization and housing donors are exempted from paying the cost of issuing a building permit, municipal and village fees, and the cost of connecting water, sewage, electricity, and gas for the residential unit allocated to the individuals covered, for one time only, in connection with the construction of housing for individuals covered by the aforementioned support organizations. The aforementioned appropriations are foreseen in the annual budget bills.
for-
1- The water required by water-based industries, except for the food, health, and drinking industries, is supplied from unconventional water (including wastewater and seawater). The Ministry of Energy is required to issue a temporary conventional water permit in cases where it is not possible to supply unconventional water, provided that there is water commensurate with the economic value of the water and products.
The executive regulations of this section and the determination of the temporary period for each license, as well as the determination of the economic value of water, are prepared by the Ministry of Energy in cooperation with the Ministries of Industry, Mines and Trade, Roads and Urban Development, and Agricultural Jihad, and are subject to approval by the Council of Ministers.
2- The Ministry of Energy is required to supervise the development, implementation, and operation of projects implemented by investors in the water and electricity sector, in line with the integrated management of water and electricity, within the framework of the system’s general policies in the fields of water and energy and the laws of “Removing Obstacles to the Development of the Electricity Industry” and “Equitable Distribution of Water”, while making maximum use of the technical and executive capacities of the non-governmental sector. The implementers of these projects are required to implement their projects and sub-projects within the framework of the technical and executive system, notified policies, and regulations of the Ministry of Energy.
The executive regulations of this section are prepared by the Ministry of Energy in coordination with the Ministry of Industry, Mines and Trade and are approved by the Council of Ministers.
C- In order to coordinate and accelerate the completion and operation of main and secondary irrigation and drainage network projects, the Ministries of Power and Agricultural Jihad are authorized to spend the approved funds of the relevant projects and domestic resources in the form of technical assistance and credit to support investors in benefit-sharing projects for irrigation and drainage networks in accordance with a model that will be approved by the Council of Ministers within six months of the entry into force of this law upon the joint proposal of the aforementioned ministries.
D- Agro-industrial companies and individuals and legal entities with irrigated lands of ten hectares or more, whether continuous or non-continuous, are required to implement new irrigation networks (surface or subsurface) for their lands by the end of the second year of the program with the support approved by the Council of Ministers in order to increase agricultural water productivity. In case of failure to implement, from the beginning of the third year of the program, the water price of the companies and individuals and legal entities in question will be charged at the highest agricultural water rate in the region. The Ministry of Agricultural Jihad is required to supervise the proper implementation of this clause.
Note 1- The implementation of this ruling is subject to the approval of the supports and their implementation.
Note 2 - The government is required to take legal action to increase agricultural water productivity, which is the subject of the general policies of the Seventh Plan, through other methods, other than those covered by this clause.
E- The Ministry of Energy is required, in cooperation with the Ministries of Industry, Mines and Trade, and Petroleum, and the Environmental Protection Organization, to take action within three months of the entry into force of this law to reallocate the water consumed by large water-absorbing industries throughout the country and to announce a schedule for providing alternative water with priority to unconventional water sources, in order to reduce water consumption in the industry and mining sector. At the end of the announced schedule, the price of conventional water delivered or withdrawn by large water-absorbing industries, if there is capacity for unconventional and alternative water sources within the area where the said industries are located, shall be determined to be equivalent to the average cost of alternative water supply projects. The resources obtained shall be deposited into the income account of the Iranian Water Resources Management Company with the National Treasury and shall be spent in proportion to the income received, on the implementation of provincial and national water and wastewater sector projects approved in the annual budget laws. Industrial towns and areas, industries and mines covered by this clause shall be given priority in receiving facilities and bidding for wastewater use.
C- In order to promote the country's water policy (diplomacy), the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is required, in cooperation with the Ministry of Energy and the Environmental Protection Organization and in coordination with the Supreme National Security Council, to formulate a document and roadmap for water policy (diplomacy) within the framework of the country's macro policy (diplomacy) and by considering the following axes. In this regard, in order to utilize all capacities, including political, economic, social, security, educational, health and international transportation, all relevant agencies must cooperate and interact with the aforementioned agencies:
1- Dynamic and flexible multi-layered policy (diplomacy) that adapts to different time and place conditions in the water sector
2- Identify and understand political factors and drivers along with other regional and international drivers affecting the country's border and shared waters at the scale of the transboundary watershed.
3- Analyzing economic opportunities and trade-offs with other opportunities in different regions, which can be discussed in negotiations related to cross-border and shared water resources.
4- Necessary technical, political, environmental and international legal solutions and measures to exercise Iran's rights to transboundary and shared water resources
5- Drawing up various possible options related to transboundary water resources and corresponding solutions for each option.
6- Identifying and determining the country's position and plan for utilizing the international capacities of bilateral treaties and agreements and international treaties (conventions) related to transboundary and shared water resources and the environment.
The Ministry of Foreign Affairs is required to submit a report on the performance of this section to the Parliament every six months.
G- The Ministry of Energy is required to complete, equip, and organize the quantitative and qualitative monitoring network of the country's water resources during the first two years of the program, utilizing up-to-date technologies, and to launch a national water accounting system under the supervision of the Supreme Water Council. The national water data reference system will be the reference for any policy-making in various departments of the country, in compliance with the National Data and Information Management Law, in cooperation with the National Meteorological Organization and water-consuming sectors.
Note - The Ministry of Energy is required, in cooperation with the Ministry of Agricultural Jihad, to prepare a methodological program for determining the water balance in line with international standards during the first two years and to update and present the water resources and consumption balance sheet every year.
The Ministry of Energy is required to submit a report on the performance of this section to the Parliament every six months.
Surface and groundwater resources
Article 40 – In order to preserve water resources, balance and control the decline in groundwater levels, and prevent over-extraction of the country's water resources, the following measures shall be taken:
A- Executive agencies, non-governmental public institutions and organizations, and the armed forces are required, in cooperation with the Ministry of Energy, to equip all water resources at their disposal with standard smart metering devices under the supervision of this Ministry in the first year of the program’s implementation and regulate their water consumption within the permissible limit announced by the said Ministry. In case of failure to comply with these duties, any withdrawal from these water resources will be considered unauthorized and the Ministry of Energy is required to deal with it within the framework of relevant laws and regulations.
Note - In conditions of water stress, with the approval of the Supreme Water Council, the aforementioned agencies and institutions are required to provide the Ministry of Energy with their water resources and lands suitable for digging drinking water wells.
B- Irrigation of green spaces using drinking water, if alternative water is available, as determined by the Ministry of Energy, is prohibited in all public and government places. Violators will be subject to the sixth degree of Ta’zir punishment as per Article (19) of the Islamic Penal Code. Municipalities and other custodians of public and government places are required to construct independent green space irrigation networks and separate them from drinking water and use wastewater and other unconventional waters in compliance with the permitted limits of environmental and health standards and indicators.
C- In order to ensure the sustainability of groundwater-related needs in critical plains, the Ministry of Energy is required to install meters on wells in coordination with the Ministries of Oil and Agricultural Jihad and in order to manage (control) over-withdrawal of water resources. In case of water withdrawal in excess of the exploitation license, after warning them twice at least one month apart, it will take action to collect a fine proportional to the percentage of over-withdrawal, up to the cost price of regional surface water, and deposit the said amount into the account of the National Treasury. In case of repeated over-withdrawal of water, exceeding forty percent (40%) of the exploitation license, the Ministry of Energy is required to temporarily cut off the water quota in the next cropping season for one cropping season.
The executive regulations of this clause will be prepared by the Ministry of Energy in cooperation with the Ministry of Agricultural Jihad and will be approved by the Council of Ministers.
The Ministry of Energy is required to submit a performance report on this section to the Agriculture, Water, Natural Resources, and Environment Committee and the Parliamentary Oversight Office every six months.
D- The Ministry of Energy, in coordination with the Ministry of Agricultural Jihad, is obliged to:
1- Within one year of the entry into force of this law, take steps to establish participatory water management by creating or strengthening user organizations as referred to in Article (5) of the Law on Increasing Productivity in the Agricultural and Natural Resources Sector, approved on 23/04/1389, in each of the country's aquifers.
2- If there are organizations mentioned in part (1) of this clause, it shall delegate its management duties in the protection and exploitation of groundwater and surface water resources, such as patrolling, inspecting and securing ecological rights of aquatic ecosystems, preventing unauthorized withdrawal of surface water resources, preventing over-withdrawal of authorized wells, measures related to blocking unauthorized wells, collecting water fees, and repairing and maintaining irrigation networks to them by concluding a contract. The Ministry of Energy shall be responsible for supervising the performance of these organizations.
The Ministry of Energy is required to submit a performance report on this section to the Agriculture, Water, Natural Resources, and Environment Committee and the Parliamentary Oversight Office every six months.
E- The movement and operation of any well drilling device with the approval of the CEO and members of the board of directors of drilling companies and the license of the Ministry of Energy, and the refusal to do so is considered a crime. The Islamic Republic of Iran’s Police Command is obliged to cooperate and prevent the movement of the aforementioned devices without a license. In case of violation of this ruling, in addition to the seizure of well drilling equipment and machinery, the natural persons who own the drilling device and, depending on the violation, the CEO and members of the board of directors of drilling companies will be subject to the punishment of Article (45) of the Fair Water Distribution Law approved on 16/12/1361 with subsequent amendments and additions by the court. Also, the activity licenses of natural and legal persons who commit the above crime more than twice will be canceled.
The Ministry of Energy is required to identify and seize illegally drilled wells in coordination with the Islamic Republic of Iran's Police Command and the Prosecutor's Office. The executive regulations of this order will be prepared by the Ministry of Energy in cooperation with the Ministry of Agricultural Jihad and will be approved by the Council of Ministers.
The Ministry of Energy is required to submit a report on the actions taken regarding this clause to the Agriculture, Water, Natural Resources, and Environment Commission and the Parliamentary Oversight Office every six months.
C- Water transfer between the six internal watersheds for non-potable uses is prohibited. Approval of water allocation and implementation of potable water transfer plans between watersheds and provinces is possible after technical procedures and approval by the Supreme Water Council, taking into account environmental needs, in accordance with the standards and permitted limits set forth in the documents and laws for the source rights.
Note: The extraction and transfer of water from the sea and lakes is not subject to the provisions of this clause.
G- The Ministry of Energy is authorized to make the necessary arrangements through the private sector until the end of the program implementation to provide, design, and build at least eighty percent (80%) of the desalination plants needed by the provinces located on the coasts of the Persian Gulf, the Sea of 
Oman, and the Caspian Sea through guaranteed purchase of desalinated water, as well as smart management and consolidation of desalination plant purchases through technology transfer to the interior, including through the Academic Jihad, universities, research centers, knowledge-based companies, and the private sector.
H- In order to stabilize the conditions of the Caspian Sea, the government is obliged to carry out the necessary studies, preparations, and measures.
Wastewater recycling
Article 41-
A- It is prohibited to release contaminated water and pollute surface and underground water resources. The perpetrator will be sentenced to the punishment stipulated in Article (688) of Book Five of the Islamic Penal Code (Penalties and Deterrent Punishments) approved on 2/3/1996 with subsequent amendments and additions.
B- The Ministry of Interior, in coordination with municipalities and rural municipalities, is required to prevent the leakage and infiltration of waste and leachate into water and soil resources through proper management of urban and rural waste.
C- In order to preserve and protect the quantity and quality of water resources, in accordance with their legal duties, the Ministry of Energy and the Environmental Protection Organization and their affiliated units are exempt from paying litigation costs in all stages of handling legal and criminal cases and lawsuits in all judicial authorities.
D- In Note (3) of the single article of the Law on Creating Facilities for the Development of Sewage Projects and Reconstruction of Urban Water Networks, after the phrase "People's Financial Participation Solutions", the phrase "By determining the relevant tariff within the ceiling of ten percent (10%) of the legal water and sewage tariff" and after the phrase "Minister of Energy", the phrase "(as Secretary of the Supreme Water Council)" is added.
Chapter 9 – Energy
Article 42 – In implementing paragraph (8) of the general policies of the Seventh Five-Year Plan and in order to achieve the following quantitative goals, action shall be taken in accordance with the provisions of this chapter:

The Ministries of Oil and Energy are required to submit annual reports on energy performance indicators (oil and gas) and energy performance indicators (electricity) to the Parliament, respectively.
Energy management system
Article 43 – The following measures shall be taken to improve the decision-making system and enhance productivity:
A- The Ministries of Oil and Energy are required, in cooperation with the organization, to reform the administrative and organizational structure of their headquarters, companies, and subordinate organizations in the fields of electricity, gas, and oil, with the approach of separating governance duties from entrepreneurship, and to submit the necessary proposal after approval by the Supreme Administrative Council for the necessary legal formalities by the end of the first year of the program's implementation.
The Ministries of Oil and Energy are required to submit a report on the performance of this clause to the Social and Energy Committees of the Parliament every six months.
B- The Ministry of Energy is required to improve the business environment of the electricity industry, increase competitiveness in this industry, and increase the share of electricity transactions in the energy market in such a way that, by supplying electricity generated by the country's power plants, the share of the aforementioned transactions will increase to at least thirty percent (30%) by the end of the second year of the program, and to at least sixty percent (60%) of the total transactions by the end of the program.
The executive regulations of this clause shall be prepared within three months of the entry into force of this law, upon the proposal of the Ministry of Energy and in cooperation with the Ministries of Oil, Economic Affairs, Finance, and Organization, and shall be approved by the Economic Council and approved by the Council of Ministers.
C- In order to strengthen the supervision of the country's nuclear and radiation facilities and activities, the country's nuclear safety system center affiliated with the Atomic Energy Organization of Iran shall be transformed into a state institution with an independent personality. All the powers, credits and properties of this center shall be transferred to the institution. The statute of this institution shall be prepared within one year of the entry into force of this law upon the proposal of the Atomic Energy Organization of Iran in cooperation with the country's administrative and employment organization and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
D- The Ministry of Oil and the Organization are required to issue the certificate of saved fuel referred to in Article (46) of this law for the fossil fuel saved by nuclear power plants constructed during the implementation of the program every month and deliver it to the Atomic Energy Organization of Iran.
Energy production and policy (diplomacy)
Article 44 – With the aim of maximum production and in line with the development of energy policy (diplomacy), presence in international markets, and strengthening the economy, the following measures will be taken:
A- The Ministry of Oil is authorized, in compliance with the laws and Article Seventy-Seven (77) of the Constitution, through the National Iranian Oil Company, to enter into joint exploitation contracts with neighbors, as well as enter into production participation contracts in joint fields, without transferring ownership in the joint fields.
B- The Ministry of Oil is authorized to participate in the development of a foreign refinery or petro-refinery, or the construction of a new foreign refinery or petro-refinery, or the acquisition of their shares, with the aim of expanding the export of petroleum products through relevant subsidiaries or non-governmental applicant companies, subject to obtaining the necessary guarantees for receiving feedstock from the Islamic Republic of Iran, and also to increase the domestic capacity of the country's petro-refining by 300,000 barrels per day, through the exchange of required services and equipment, in compliance with the Law on Supporting the Development of Downstream Crude Oil and Gas Condensate Industries Using Public Investment, approved on 24/04/1398, with subsequent amendments and additions, from the point of delivery of crude oil in excess of public budget obligations, by including it in the ceiling of resources and expenditures of the annual budget laws with the approval of the Economic Council.
C- The Ministry of Petroleum is obliged to:
1- Through the relevant subsidiary in gas affairs and from the internal resources of the aforementioned company as well as the resources of the "Oil and Gas Investment" account, and by attracting the participation of the private sector, take steps to create and develop the necessary infrastructure for storing natural gas, including underground and surface reservoirs, in such a way that at the end of the program, the production rate from the natural gas storage site during the two-month peak consumption period increases to at least one hundred and twenty million cubic meters of natural gas per day.
2- To the extent determined in the annual budget bills, from the internal resources of its subsidiaries and the oil and gas investment account, by the end of the second year of the program at the latest, by launching and operating a comprehensive smart energy management system to monitor and supervise the flow and processes of the extraction, transmission, storage, production and consumption points (domestic and export) of the following goods: 1) crude oil, gas condensates and gas (sour and sweet) 2) main, special and by-products of petroleum 3) gas products 4) petrochemical products and derivatives with two structures: 1- "Information and data bank" 2- "Installation of smart electronic mass measuring devices" in pipelines and all channels and warehouses of the country's oil industry, to make arrangements to enable real-time monitoring and the amount in the flow of the above-mentioned goods from harvesting to consumption in pipelines and all tanks and warehouses. The Ministry of Oil is required to submit a monthly performance report on the implementation of this paragraph to the Energy Commission and the Commission on Article Ninety (90) of the Constitution of the Majlis.
Those who refuse to implement this part will be sentenced to the second to fifth degree of Ta'zir punishment as per Article (19) of the Islamic Penal Code, in proportion to their refusal or obstruction of implementation. In addition to the aforementioned punishment, if the system is not implemented, from the third year of implementation of the program, the equivalent of five out of ten thousand of the value of all transactions will be deposited from the internal resources of the relevant subsidiaries into the "Energy Consumption Optimization" account.
D- In the implementation of paragraph (10) of the general policies of the Seventh Five-Year Plan, in order to transform Iran into a regional energy hub, with the aim of achieving the country's gas export and import volumes of forty billion cubic meters and twenty billion cubic meters per year, respectively, swap services for petroleum products and crude oil from the Commonwealth of Independent States at the rate of two hundred thousand barrels per day, and the country's electricity exchange at the rate of at least twenty billion kilowatt hours per year, a regional energy trade steering committee shall be formed within six months of the entry into force of this law. This headquarters is formed under the chairmanship of the President (in his absence, the First Vice President) and with the membership of the Ministers of Foreign Affairs, Oil, and Energy, and one member of the Energy Commission elected by the Parliament as an observer member. In addition to compiling a document and roadmap for regional energy policy (diplomacy), including a list of target countries, it takes decisions on matters related to export, import, swap services, and energy transit (gas, electricity, oil, and oil products) contracts in accordance with the seventy-seventh (77) and one hundred and twenty-fifth (125) principles of the Constitution and within the framework of the laws.
The Ministry of Petroleum is required to submit a report on the performance of this article to the Parliament every six months.
Article 45 - In order to increase the added value of products in the downstream petrochemical chain, as well as to increase the quality of petroleum products and their compliance with domestic and international legal standards and requirements, the government is required to prepare the necessary mechanisms to improve the quality of manufactured products and reduce the production of heavy products in such a way that by the end of the program, the composition and quality of petroleum products produced by oil refining and petrochemical companies meet the necessary standards.
Note - In order to ensure the completion of the oil and gas industry value chain, a five percent (5%) discount on feedstock for oil and gas condensate refining companies, as well as a discount on feedstock delivered to existing petrochemical companies (the difference between the price of delivered feedstock and the obligation stipulated in the Law on Targeting Subsidies, approved on 15/10/1388, with subsequent amendments and additions), is conditional on allocating at least forty percent (40%) of the annual net profit of these companies to a special capital reserve account for the quality improvement and development of the downstream chain of the same company. The executive regulations of this article shall be prepared by the Ministry of Petroleum in cooperation with the Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance and the Environmental Protection Organization and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
Energy consumption
Article 46 – In order to manage and reduce energy intensity, the following measures shall be taken:
one thousand-
1- In order to eliminate energy imbalances and increase the share of renewable energies in the country's electricity supply, the Ministries of Oil, Power, Industry, Mines and Trade, and the Interior are required, within the framework of Article (12) of the Law on Removing Barriers to Competitive Production and Improving the Country's Financial System, to take the necessary measures to develop the construction of solar and wind power plants, self-sufficient power plants in the small and medium-sized industrial, agricultural, commercial, public, administrative and household sectors, electrification of vehicles with priority for city buses, taxis, and motorcycles, and to provide cooling and heating for buildings in the southern coastal provinces of the country using geothermal heat pumps.
2- In order to establish cross-sectoral coordination and centralized macro-management in the field of energy consumption optimization, optimal management of energy imbalances in various sectors, taking into account considerations of reducing energy intensity, and following up on the implementation of energy optimization plans in the energy supply and consumption sectors, and determining the amount and method of allocating all energy subsidies in each sector by fully implementing the Subsidies Targeting Law, the government is required to establish the “Energy Optimization and Strategic Management Organization” under the supervision of the President, subject to his approval of the consolidation and integration of organizational capacities existing in the Fuel Consumption Optimization Company, the Renewable Energy and Electricity Efficiency Organization (SATBA), and the Transportation and Fuel Management Headquarters, and to have its statute approved by the Council of Ministers within three months. In order to facilitate the formation of the “energy optimization market,” ensure the settlement of “energy saving certificates,” and reduce their default, the government must establish an “Energy Consumption Optimization Account” with the National Treasury within a maximum of six months from the entry into force of this law with the following resources:
1-2- Government obligations in repayment of energy consumption optimization projects, subject to the expenditure table in Note (14) of the annual budget (annual equivalent of one percent (1%) of resources derived from crude oil exports, gas condensates, and net natural gas exports)
2-2- Five percent (5%) annually of the profits of the subsidiaries of the Ministries of Oil and Energy
3.2- All fees received from the loss of flare gases
4-2- Fines received under Article (26) and revenues from fuel savings under Article (61) of the Law on Reforming the Energy Consumption Pattern, approved on 4/12/1389, with subsequent amendments and additions.
5.2- Ten percent (10%) of the revenues from the export and domestic sales of all gas by-products, including ethane, propane, butane, pentane, and sulfur, as well as gas liquids, of the subsidiaries of the Ministry of Oil.
6-2- Other resources foreseen in annual budget bills for optimizing energy consumption
7-2- At least thirty percent (30%) of the government's share of the revenues from energy savings in accordance with the mechanism of paragraph "P" of this article, which is paid by the government.
Note 1- The use of resources from this account is permitted solely for the guaranteed purchase of energy saving or fuel-free certificates submitted by the public and the government and non-government sectors at a minimum price equivalent to fifty percent (50%) of the highest domestic approved price of each energy carrier included in the certificate, and is prohibited for any other uses, including cost credits and acquisition of capital assets.
Note 2 - The government is authorized to take the necessary legal action to convert the aforementioned account into a fund.
The executive regulations of this clause shall be prepared by the organization in cooperation with the Ministries of Petroleum, Energy, and Economic Affairs and Finance within three months of the entry into force of this law and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
for-
1- In order to eliminate the gasoline imbalance, create diversity in the country's fuel basket, and implement the passive defense tasks and the Clean Air Law approved on 25/04/1396, the organization is required, in cooperation with the Ministries of Oil, Interior, Industry, Mines and Trade, the Environmental Protection Organization, and the National Organization of Standards of Iran, to prepare a comprehensive plan for the supply and allocation of energy carriers for the country's transportation network, including gasoline, oil, gas, liquefied natural gas, electricity, and compressed natural gas, within a maximum of six months from the entry into force of this law, and submit it to the approval of the Council of Ministers.
2- From the beginning of the second year of the program, the subsidiary of the Ministry of Oil is required to design and implement a mechanism whereby the oil and gas credit quota is allocated only at stations located on the routes related to the online electronic waybill and based on the distance and performance approved by the Ministries of Roads and Urban Development and the Interior and can be used for the relevant vehicle. Oil and gas consumption at other stations or more than the quota is subject to an incremental-stepwise rate adjustment in compliance with the laws. The Ministries of Roads and Urban Development and the Interior and the Police Command of the Islamic Republic of Iran (FARACA) are required to provide the subsidiary of the Ministry of Oil with online access to intercity and intracity electronic waybills and the identity of the vehicle owner by the end of the first year of the program.
The executive regulations of this section will be prepared by the Ministry of Petroleum in cooperation with the Ministries of Roads and Urban Development and the Interior within a maximum of six months and will be approved by the Council of Ministers.
C- In order to popularize energy consumption optimization and develop the energy optimization market, the "Energy Optimization and Strategic Management Organization" is required to notify the relevant subsidiaries of the Ministries of Oil and Power to issue certificates of energy savings during peak and off-peak consumption (electricity or natural gas), in energy consumption optimization projects for the benefit of the investor, the saving factor, commensurate with the energy consumption optimization goals of this program, in accordance with the energy and environmental optimization market mechanism through the energy market (exchange) under the following conditions:
1- Certificates are anonymous, transferable, and can be bought and sold on the energy market. The certificate can be used to settle one’s own and others’ energy bills and to pay taxes for energy-consuming companies up to the company’s energy consumption price. Certificate transactions are not subject to value-added tax and are collected only from the recipient of the energy carrier at the time of delivery of the energy carrier specified in the certificate.
2- Those household, public and commercial non-production subscribers (consumers) who have reduced their energy consumption compared to their consumption in the previous year in the same period, as well as those industrial or commercial production subscribers who have reduced their energy consumption compared to their consumption in the previous year in the same period, through adjustments related to production performance, are eligible to receive a certificate at least equivalent to the "energy saved". In the event of a consumer's request and commitment to save energy in a specific period of time in the future, a conditional certificate is issued to his benefit after the request is approved and before the savings are realized. In the event that the savings are not realized, the price of the energy carrier quantities committed by the consumer is calculated at the price on the day of the certificate, and the consumer is obligated to settle it. Also, governmental and non-governmental legal entities are allowed to receive the certificates subject to this section on behalf of energy consumers, based on the mechanism determined by the "Organization for Optimization and Strategic Energy Management" and based on valid contracts with energy consumers.
3- In the case of energy consumption optimization plans(projects), the “Energy Optimization and Strategic Management Organization” is required to enter into contracts with governmental and non-governmental investors and, by issuing a certificate, repay a portion of the principal and subsidiary capital through the “Energy Consumption Optimization Account” if each unit of the work subject to the optimization plans is completed. The maximum time for the aforementioned organization to announce the results of the verification of the work subject to the contract for this component is six months after the investor’s request. If the results are not announced within the specified period, this organization is required to pay the investment cost made through the “Energy Consumption Optimization Account” upon the investor’s request and in accordance with the arrangements specified in the regulations. The government is authorized to issue savings certificates in accordance with the mechanism specified in this article, at the request of investors in the projects of Article (12) of the Law on Removing Barriers to Competitive Production and Improving the Country’s Financial System, to the extent determined in the annual budget.
The regulations of this section, including amendments to the regulations for establishing an energy and environmental optimization market, shall be prepared by the Energy Optimization and Strategic Management Organization in cooperation with the organization, the ministries of petroleum, energy, economic affairs and finance, industry, mining and trade, roads and urban development, and the Central Bank within three months of the entry into force of this law and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
The Energy Optimization and Strategic Management Organization is required to submit a report on the actions taken to the Economic and Energy Committees of the Parliament every six months.
D- Based on the approvals of the Economic Council in each of the energy saving projects subject to Article (12) of the Law on Removing Barriers to Competitive Production and Improving the Country's Financial System, the National Iranian Oil Company is authorized to provide a transfer or deposit of crude oil convertible into a certificate equivalent to the carrier saved from the government's share to investors and guarantee the delivery of oil or its equivalent value on the day of delivery.
The executive regulations of this clause shall be prepared upon the proposal of the Ministry of Petroleum and in cooperation with the Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance, the Central Bank, and the Organization, and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
E- The fines referred to in Article (26) of the Law on Reforming the Energy Consumption Pattern shall be levied based on the export price, and also the fees for flare gases burned in oil and gas facilities shall be levied per cubic meter of gas, as announced monthly by the Secretariat of the Supreme Council for Supervision of Petroleum Resources (the Organization), for the first year at five percent (5%) and until the end of the program at seventy-five percent (75%) based on the average weighted export price of natural gas, and shall be deposited from the domestic resources of the subsidiaries of the Ministry of Oil into the energy consumption optimization account referred to in subparagraph (2) of paragraph "A" of this article. Flare gases that are technically impossible to collect, as determined by the Secretariat of the Supreme Council for Supervision of Petroleum Resources (the Organization), and up to a maximum volume of three billion cubic meters per year, shall be exempt from the scope of this ruling. The executive regulations of this paragraph shall be prepared by the Organization in cooperation with the Ministry of Oil, the Organization for Optimization and Strategic Management of Energy, and the Ministries of Oil, Industry, Mines, and Trade, and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
The Ministry of Oil and the organization are required to submit a report on the actions taken to the Parliament's Energy Committee every six months.
Table No. (10) - Quantitative goals for reducing energy consumption

The Ministry of Petroleum is required to submit the performance indicators report in Table (10) to the Parliament annually.
Chapter 10 – Industrial, Mining and Production Growth Plans
Article 47 – In implementing paragraphs (8) and (9) of the general policies of the Seventh Five-Year Plan and in order to achieve the following quantitative goals, action shall be taken in accordance with the provisions of this law:
Table No. (11) - Quantitative targets for industry, mining and production growth performance indicators
