B- The Ministry of Communications and Information Technology is required to provide the necessary bandwidth and facilities for the general public to access national media networks and programs in all parts of the country on the basis of the national information network, as well as maximum access at the international level.
C- The Islamic Republic of Iran Broadcasting Organization and the Ministry of Culture and Islamic Guidance are required to take the necessary legal action in order to support Islamic-Iranian culture and values 
and develop media governance, as well as considering the responsibility of those agencies in regulating regulations, issuing licenses in compliance with the Law on Facilitating the Issuance of Business Licenses, and supervising media active in the field of comprehensive audio and video, in preparing a table of financial violations, the method of supporting and addressing violations by individuals in the above cases.
Note - The Islamic Republic of Iran Broadcasting Organization and the Ministry of Culture and Islamic Guidance, within the scope of their stated duties and authorities (in the field of production, distribution of products, issuing licenses and how to supervise them), are subject to their own specific laws and regulations, in compliance with Articles (1) and (7) of the Law on the Implementation of General Policies, Article 44 (44) of the amended Constitution of 15/11/2019, and also in compliance with the "Division of Work and Determination of the Limits of Duties of the Islamic Republic of Iran Broadcasting Organization and the Ministry of Culture and Islamic Guidance" in accordance with the regulations approved by the Supreme Council of the Cultural Revolution, as the case may be.
Article 78–
A- In order to develop public and championship sports, the Islamic Republic of Iran Broadcasting Organization is required, in coordination with the Ministry of Sports and Youth, to prepare regulations on how to determine the amount of television broadcasting rights for sports competitions and how to secure and distribute them among the beneficiaries, taking into account the quality and quantity of competitions and the number of audiences, within three months of the entry into force of this law, and submit them to the Council of Ministers for approval.
B- In order to promote economic health, financial monitoring (control) system and sustainable investment progress in clubs, the Ministry of Sports and Youth is required to prepare fair play financial guidelines in cooperation with federations that have professional teams (leagues) and submit them to the general assembly of the relevant federations for approval within a maximum of six months.
C- According to Article (6) of the Law on the Objectives, Duties and Authorities of the Ministry of Sports and Youth approved on June 16, 2020, the Fund for the Protection of Sports Champions and Veterans, as the custodian of social insurance for athletes and champions, is obliged to pay the social insurance premiums of the above individuals from the resources at its disposal and the income of the subsidiary companies of this Fund until retirement, in compliance with Clause "X" of Article (28) of this Law.
D- In order to develop the sports economy and attract and encourage non-governmental sector sponsors to work in the country's sports field, the expenditure equivalent to one hundred percent (100%) of the aforementioned persons in order to help realize the programs of the Ministry of Sports and Youth, the National Olympic and Paralympic Committees, and sports federations in line with the quantitative and qualitative development of development infrastructure, holding and participating in national and international sports events, solely with regard to the issue of expenditure credits and acquisition of capital assets stipulated in the annual budget laws, upon the proposal of the Ministry of Sports and Youth and the approval of the organization in accordance with the regulations prepared by the Ministry of Sports and Youth and the Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance and approved by the Council of Ministers, shall be considered as a tax credit for the aforementioned persons and shall be deductible annually at the rate of one percent (1%) from the income tax of the aforementioned persons as a collective expense after accounting with the National Treasury.
E- The organization is required to allocate twenty-seven hundredths of one percent (0.27%) of the total nine percent (9%) of the value-added tax during the implementation of the program for organizing youth affairs and promoting and generalizing physical activity and popularizing sports. This amount is foreseen in the lines related to the ministries of sports and youth at the rate of sixty percent (60%) and education at the rate of forty percent (40%) in the annual budget laws and is paid directly from the treasury to these ministries.
Note 1- This credit is only spent in the provinces.
Note 2- Any payment of any kind from this location to professional sports is prohibited and constitutes illegal appropriation of government funds and property.
The organization and the Ministries of Sports and Youth, and Education are required to submit a report on the performance of this section to the Education, Research and Technology, and Culture Committees of the Parliament every six months.
Chapter 16 – Women, Family and Population
Article 79 - Action shall be taken to implement paragraphs (15) and (16) of the general policies of the Seventh Plan and to achieve the following quantitative objectives in accordance with the provisions of this chapter:
Table No. (17) - Quantitative objectives of women, family and population performance indicators
Performance measure	Quantitative target at the end of the program compared to the base year (1402)
Promoting correct patterns of spouse selection and encouraging timely, easy, and sustainable marriages in accordance with Islamic-Iranian culture and local capacities (in the form of holding workshops and training courses)	25% growth
Increasing women's job skills (through workshops and training courses)	25% growth
Specialized centers for family counseling, marriage and divorce prevention	25% growth
Decreasing average age of marriage	1 year
Increase in the marriage rate relative to the population of marriageable age	5 percent
Reducing the ratio of registered divorces to the married population	5 percent
Total fertility rate	2.5 children
Increasing the share of innovation acceleration infrastructures in the field of women and family compared to other infrastructures (including knowledge-based companies, creative and innovation houses, creative and innovative institutions in the field of women, family and children)	10 percent
Reducing illegal abortions	30 percent
The Presidential Vice President for Women and Family Affairs is required to submit an annual report on the performance indicators of women, families, and populations to the parliament.
Article 80–
A- In order to strengthen the institution of the family, the government is required to organize marriage and family counseling centers and the activities of legally licensed marriage and family psychologists from agencies under the executive branch with the aim of promoting the correct model of spouse selection, encouraging timely and lasting marriage, and also reducing divorce. It is also required to take the necessary legal measures regarding the following matters during the years of implementation of the program:
1- Organizing and accrediting counseling centers in accordance with Islamic culture
2- Organizing, integrating, and creating a system for evaluating the qualifications and ranking of consultants
3- Promoting counseling before, during and after marriage for at least five years.
The executive regulations of this clause will be prepared by the Vice Presidency for Women and Family Affairs in cooperation with the Ministry of Sports and Youth, the National Welfare Organization, and the Organization of the Psychology and Counseling System of the Islamic Republic of Iran, in consultation with the management of the seminaries, during the first year of the program, and will be approved by the Council of Ministers.
B- In order to understand the developments in the field of women and family, increase the efficiency of related measures and policies, amend laws and regulations, and improve the governance system in order to promote family-centeredness and strengthen the approach of the Iranian-Islamic model of women (the third model), the Vice Presidency for Women and Family Affairs, in cooperation with relevant agencies and research and think tanks, and with the opinion of the Seminary Management Center, while observing the approvals, duties, and authorities of the Supreme Council of the Cultural Revolution, is required to determine indicators for measuring the status of women and family, prepare an atlas of the field of women and family, and conduct future research on issues in this field in the first year of the program.
Note 1- The Ministry of Interior, in cooperation with the Presidential Assistant for Women and Family Affairs, the Ministry of Culture and Islamic Guidance, and the Secretariat of the National Headquarters of the Jamiat, is required to conduct national surveys based on the indicators collected in the field of women, family, and population in the first and last years of the program and to make the results available to the relevant agencies and institutions and the Cultural Commission of the Parliament.
Note 2 - Given the need to clarify the dimensions of the Islamic Revolution discourse and demands in the field of women and family in the international arena, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, in cooperation with the Presidential Vice President for Women and Family Affairs and the Islamic Culture and Communications Organization, is required to take action in various dimensions, including propaganda and enlightening measures regarding the active role of women in Iran and Islamic societies.
C- The Ministry of Cooperation, Labor and Social Welfare is required to take the following measures in cooperation with the Presidential Assistant for Women and Family Affairs, the Imam Khomeini Relief Committee (RA), and the organization in order to empower and support female heads of households and female heads of households:
1- Designing indicators to assess the status of households headed by women and abusive parents from an economic, social, cultural, and health (physical and mental) perspective, and leveling support and services based on age, physical, and capacity requirements in the first six months of the program, and continuously monitoring the status of those covered by this clause.
2- Launching the Service Unit Window System in the first year of program implementation in order to integrate the process of identification, recruitment, and support services and empower support and public institutions in the field of female heads of households and abusive caregivers based on service stratification in compliance with the National Data and Information Management Law.
3- Developing legal measures to reduce by fifty percent (50%) the tariff for consulting services under the National Welfare Organization and the Ministry of Sports and Youth for families headed by a woman or an abusive parent.
4- Supporting and strengthening the capacity of jihadi groups and NGOs in the field of empowering households headed by women and abusive parents.
Note - The Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare is required to report annually to the Social Commission of the Parliament the performance report on the implementation of this clause and the rate of withdrawal of service recipients from the support services process.
D- In line with the implementation of paragraph (13) of the general family policies and the general policies of the Seventh Plan with the aim of preventing social harms and social discipline, strengthening the family institution, and monitoring (controlling) and reducing divorce, the Ministry of Interior is obliged to:
1- Amend and complete the "National Program for Controlling and Reducing Divorce and the Social Discipline Program" within three months of the entry into force of this law based on the following:
1-1- Prioritizing important elements affecting divorce in terms of social, cultural, and economic aspects, as well as social discipline
2.1- Planning before, during and after divorce
2- With a focus on reducing the divorce index by five percent (5%) and using the funds foreseen in its annual budget bills, it should launch a system to evaluate the performance of the institutions and the effectiveness of counseling during divorce, as well as training before, during and after marriage, and to review other government measures aimed at reducing divorce, as well as monitoring the status and causes of divorce in the country based on data from the judiciary and demographic, economic, social and cultural variables, in compliance with the National Data and Information Management Law, within one year of the entry into force of this law.
E- The Ministry of Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare, in cooperation with the National Administrative and Employment Organization and the Presidential Vice-President for Women and Family Affairs, is required to prepare regulations and executive mechanisms for the women's employment program, respecting the role of women in the family, and determining the duties and functions of each of the executive agencies, within one year of the entry into force of this law for approval by the Council of Ministers.
Article 81 - In order to support the family and promote the efficiency of the organizational structure in the areas of family, women, and youth, and provide comprehensive support for childbearing, remove obstacles, create effective incentives, and reform culture, the following measures shall be taken:
A- With the aim of strengthening the family institution and creating favorable conditions for the restoration of women's material and spiritual rights, focusing on institutionalizing the Muslim woman model (the third model), the government shall take legal action to reorganize and improve the structure and organization of the women and family sector, including the structure of the Presidential Women and Family Affairs Office and the structure of the Women and Family Affairs Advisors of the executive agencies, in order to improve and strengthen the executive leadership of policies and laws in the women and family sector, monitor the agencies and laws in the women and family sector, and create coherence between the Presidential Women and Family Affairs Office and the Women and Family Affairs Advisors of the executive agencies. The Presidential Women and Family Affairs Office is required to submit a report on the performance of this section to the Parliament every six months.
B- The Ministry of Education (National Organization for Child Education) is required to take action, in compliance with the approvals of the Supreme Council of the Cultural Revolution, to develop a program to diversify kindergarten models, including home kindergartens, mother-child homes, and institutional kindergartens (affiliated with government and public institutions), while respecting their non-governmental nature, their management and supervision criteria, and each educational guideline on a specific basis, and to submit it to the Council of Ministers for approval within six months of the entry into force of this law.
C- In line with the implementation of the general policies of the Seventh Five-Year Plan and the implementation of the Law on Protection of the Family and Youth of the Population, the Ministry of Health, Treatment and Medical Education, in cooperation with the Secretariat of the National Headquarters of the Population, the Academic Jihad, and the Vice Presidency for Women and Family Affairs, is required to implement, within three months of the entry into force of this law, a program to organize new alternative methods in the field of infertility, including surrogacy and egg freezing, organize centers providing these services after obtaining the opinion of the Center for the Management of Seminaries and observing it in jurisprudence in accordance with the opinion of the Supreme Leader, within the annual budget ceiling (sources of the Law on Protection of the Family and Youth of the Population), and make legal arrangements for basic insurance coverage, and submit it to the approval of the Council of Ministers.
Note - The possibility of freezing eggs and benefiting from the related basic insurance also includes unmarried girls over the age of thirty.
D- Expenses incurred by legal entities on the production of cultural and educational content on the subject of supporting the family and the youth of the population and reflecting the capacities and capabilities of the provinces and underprivileged and deprived regions in the form of documentary production, television series (serials), television films and animations, which are supervised and approved by the Islamic Republic of Iran Broadcasting Organization based on combined indicators for broadcasting on the organization's national, provincial and international networks, as well as documentaries and motion pictures that are approved by the Ministry of Culture and Islamic Guidance, are considered acceptable tax expenses.
E- The Presidential Vice-President for Science, Technology and Knowledge-Based Economy is required to work with relevant agencies to remove obstacles and facilitate childbearing and parenting for mothers, especially housewives, and to empower creative and innovative women in order to strengthen their social presence through the development of creative and innovative centers for mothers and children and increasing the share of infrastructures to accelerate innovation in the field of women and families.
Chapter 17 – Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts
Article 82 – In implementing paragraph (17) of the general policies of the Seventh Five-Year Plan and in order to achieve the following quantitative goals, action shall be taken in accordance with the provisions of this chapter and in compliance with the principles of Sharia:
Table No. (18) - Quantitative objectives of performance indicators for cultural heritage, tourism and handicrafts
Performance measure	One known	Base year 1401	Quantitative goal at the end of the program
Number of tourists entering the country	A thousand people	۴.۲۳۰ 	۱۵.۰۰۰
Number of hotels in the country	Number	۱.۴۳۰ 	۱.۹۰۰
Active museums in the country (ministries, other agencies and non-governmental)	Number	۷۷۵ 	۱۰۰۰
A work registered in the World Heritage List	Effect	۴۷ 	۵۷
Number of immovable works restored during the year	Effect	۶۰۰ 	۹۵۰
Export value of handicrafts, hand-woven carpets and related industries (based on statistics from the Islamic Republic of Iran Customs)	Million euros	۲۲۴ 	۴۹۰
Annual economic growth of handicrafts, hand-woven carpets and related industries	Percentage		۸%
Increasing the number of employees in the field of handicrafts, hand-woven carpets, and related industries	Person	۵۰۰.۰۰۰ 	1 million
The Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts is required to submit a performance report on the performance indicators in Table No. (18) to the Parliament annually.
Article 83 – In order to develop domestic tourism and increase the attraction of foreign tourists, preserve the country's cultural heritage, and also develop and promote handicrafts, the following measures shall be taken:
one thousand-
1- All tourism and handicraft facilities and activities shall have prior tax exemptions and the laws and regulations of their respective industries and shall be exempt from the laws of the guild system. In order to unify, integrate, and consolidate professional organizations in the tourism and handicraft industries, the executive regulations of this clause, including the manner of formation, administration, activities, training, and empowerment of members of the aforementioned organizations and non-governmental affairs that may be assigned to them, shall be prepared by the Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism, and Handicrafts based on laws and regulations within three months of the entry into force of this law and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
2- Subsidies and financial facilities within the framework of the annual budget and tax and duty exemptions are allocated to Irantourist and tourism facilities within the framework of relevant laws and in compliance with Article (27) of this law.
3- The infrastructure required for tourism areas, such as roads, welfare and accommodation services, will be created by utilizing the private sector's capacity for investment, providing low-cost facilities, and other support measures in the form of annual budgets.
4- All individuals active in the field of tourism and handicrafts shall obtain the necessary licenses in compliance with the Law on Facilitating the Issuance of Business Licenses through the National Window of Smart Government Services.
5- Hand-woven carpets and related industries are also subject to the provisions of this paragraph, and the Ministry of Industry, Mines and Trade continues to be responsible for carrying out related matters.
B- The necessary license for importing tourist ships, recreational vessels, vehicles and special tourism equipment for investors from the private and cooperative sectors applying for exemption from entry fees shall be issued by the Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts in compliance with the legal authority of the Ministry of Roads and Urban Development in compliance with the Law on Facilitating the Issuance of Business Licenses. The list of examples subject to this paragraph shall be determined by the Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts in cooperation with the Ministries of Industry, Mines, Trade and Roads and Urban Development within three months of the entry into force of this law. The aforementioned examples shall be distinguished by a special plate or badge by the Police Command of the Islamic Republic of Iran or the relevant legal authority and shall be used exclusively in the field of tourism services for at least ten years. Supervision of the use of vehicles and obtaining the necessary guarantees in cooperation with the Police Command of the Islamic Republic of Iran and relevant supervisory agencies shall be the responsibility of the Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts.
The executive regulations of this paragraph shall be prepared within the framework of laws and regulations within three months of the entry into force of this law and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
C- The government is obligated to take the following measures to protect cultural heritage and compensate people for their property rights:
1- The National Real Estate and Documents Registration Organization is required, in cooperation with the Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts, to digitize maps of the area and boundaries of national monuments and the boundaries of historical structures in cadastral maps, as well as the layer of cities and buildings and the boundaries of historical-cultural structures in the "Comprehensive System for Issuing Ownership Documents and an Integrated Platform for Institutional Inquiry" by the end of the second year of the program, in compliance with the National Data and Information Management Law.
The Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts is required to submit a performance report of this component to the Parliament's Cultural Commission every six months.
2- The Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts is required to review the boundaries of previously registered works and determine the boundaries of new registered works, while simultaneously observing the preservation of the work, not imposing inappropriate restrictions outside of legal authority, how to compensate for legally established restrictions for owners, and determine physical, landscape, structural, and functional boundaries, taking into account components such as height, shape (form), materials and architectural style, factors affecting the structure and stability of the work (surface and subsurface), use and methods of peripheral activities, and the possibility of future development and renovation within the boundaries, while respecting the Sharia rights of endowed places, mosques, and similar cases, including preserving the use and intentions of the donors, as well as compensating the people's property rights, including granting compensated lands to property owners located in the area and boundaries of national works who have faced restrictions and a decrease in the value of their properties.
3- The Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts is required to determine and notify the privacy of each work within a maximum of three months after its national or global registration in accordance with the relevant laws and regulations. The determination of the privacy of registered works that do not have privacy or the review of previously determined privacy during the program must be such that twenty percent (20%) of their privacy is notified in each year of the program.
D- In order to facilitate investment processes and meet the advisory and implementation needs of tourism and handicraft projects and activities, the Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts can issue licenses for “developer”, “investment facilitator” and “exploitation in the fields of tourism and handicrafts” to qualified institutions in compliance with the Law on Facilitating the Issuance of Business Licenses. These institutions are allowed to operate in matters related to the investment and exploitation process and the management of tourism facilities and institutions and the quantitative and qualitative development of handicraft production and supply, in compliance with the regulations, criteria and guidelines issued.
Note - The Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts is required to take action, directly or with the participation of the private sector, to restore and exploit historical buildings.
E- The Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts is required, in cooperation with the Ministry of Roads and Urban Development and other relevant agencies, in compliance with the Law on Facilitating the Issuance of Business Permits, to organize the issuance of permits for the creation of tourism projects with mixed use (commercial or administrative or residential or tourism) and to provide the possibility of selling and pre-selling facilities and units based on the approved plan, within the boundaries and boundaries of cities and villages by obtaining permits from the relevant executive agencies only on lands with tourism use included in the comprehensive and detailed city plans or village master plans, taking into account the establishment of necessary incentives within the framework of the laws in determining tariffs for all uses of a combined plan.
The implementing regulations for this clause shall be prepared by the Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts, in cooperation with the Ministry of Roads and Urban Development and the Islamic Revolution Housing Foundation, within a maximum of three months from the date of entry into force of this law, and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
The Ministries of Roads and Urban Development, Cultural Heritage, Tourism, and Handicrafts are required to submit reports on the performance of this section to the Civil and Cultural Commissions of the Parliament.
C- In order to facilitate, encourage and create integrated and centralized management and accelerate the development of investment in the coastal and marine tourism sector by the private and cooperative sectors, in compliance with laws and regulations, all decisions for the implementation of tourism projects, including issuing licenses through the National Business Licenses Portal, responding to inquiries, the process and contracts for the assignment of coastal and marine areas, and the use of existing piers for mixed tourism or passenger use in compliance with the Law on Facilitating the Issuance of Business Licenses, shall be delegated to a council in each coastal province chaired by the Minister of Interior or his representative who meets the necessary Sharia requirements, including trustworthiness and honesty, and with the membership of the Head of the Environmental Protection Organization or his representative who meets the necessary Sharia requirements, including trustworthiness and honesty, and with the membership of the governors, general managers of cultural heritage, tourism and handicrafts (secretary), natural resources and watershed management, ports and maritime affairs and environmental protection of the province, and the head of the Lifesaving and Diving Federation of the Islamic Republic of Iran, without the right to vote.
G- The Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts is obliged to deposit all specific income and public donations and donations from legal and natural persons, as well as income from historical and tourist sites and areas, except for endowed or similar places and museums under the supervision of this Ministry, and income from the sale of handicraft products and traditional arts produced in government workshops, into an account opened with the National Treasury. One hundred percent (100%) of the funds obtained shall be made available to the Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts to be spent on the management, development and restoration of the same sites and workshops, in accordance with paragraph "d" of Article (28) of the Law on the Addition of Certain Articles to the Law on the Regulation of Part of the Government Financial Regulations (2) approved on 4/12/1393.
The intention of the payer must be observed in the use, consumption, and expenditure of public donations and donations from natural and legal persons.
H- The Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts, in cooperation with the Ministry of Culture and Islamic Guidance, is required to take the necessary measures in various countries, in extensive interaction with personalities, institutions and religious centers of countries around the world, to ensure the presence of pilgrims and tourists seeking to learn about the Islamic Revolution and the investment of believers from different countries in the holy places and recreational areas of Iran, so that by the end of the five-year plan, the number of pilgrims and tourists in these areas will reach two and a half times that of the first year of the plan.
X- The Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts, in cooperation with the Foundation for the Preservation of Monuments and the Propagation of the Values 
of Sacred Defense and the Ministry of Culture and Islamic Guidance, is required to register at least one hundred and fifty points related to the Islamic Revolution, such as the birthplaces and deaths of the heroes and great figures of the Islamic Revolution, the Sacred Defense, and their great epic battlefields, and places related to important events in the history of the Islamic Revolution, in the list of national monuments, and by widely disseminating information about these points and environmental guidelines, it will encourage pilgrims and tourists to visit these places using all capacities, including Iranian graduates in universities abroad, foreign graduates of Iranian universities and seminaries, and graduates of the World Mustafa Community.
D- The Ministry of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts is required to prepare a "Comprehensive Document for the Management of the Production, Distribution, Supply and Export Chain of Handicrafts" within a maximum of three months from the entry into force of this law, in compliance with the approvals of the Supreme Council of the Cultural Revolution, in order to secure the value chain and improve the conditions for the production and supply of handicraft products, and in compliance with local considerations, compatibility with the authenticity of identity, promotion of the Iranian-Islamic lifestyle, and a technological approach, and submit it for approval by the Council of Ministers.
Note 1- The document subject to this paragraph must guarantee annual growth in the handicraft sector of at least eight percent (8%).
Note 2 - All agencies subject to Article (5) of the Civil Service Management Law that are subordinate to the executive branch and municipalities will be required to comply with the policies and priorities based on the needs assessment conducted in this document.
In order to develop, deepen and promote the culture of pilgrimage and to make coordinated decisions on cultural, social, infrastructural and infrastructure matters related to pilgrim affairs (domestic and foreign), the Ministry of Culture and Islamic Guidance is required to take legal action within six months of the entry into force of this law, in coordination with the Ministries of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts, Interior, Roads and Urban Development, Foreign Affairs, Economic Affairs and Finance, and Health, Treatment and Medical Education, to prepare a comprehensive pilgrimage program including facilitating pilgrimage, cultural and social affairs of pilgrims, obtaining the opinion of the Seminary Management Center, and improving and upgrading the necessary infrastructure, in compliance with the duties of the Supreme Council for Cultural Heritage and Tourism, the duties of the representatives of the Supreme Leader and the guardianship of the holy shrines of the holy sites, and the statutes of the Supreme Leader’s Representative Area in Hajj and pilgrimage matters.
The government is also required to prepare a comprehensive document on Hajj and pilgrimage by the end of the first year of the program, in cooperation with the representative of the Supreme Leader in Hajj, and take the necessary legal action to implement it.
Chapter 18 – Domestic Policy and Social Health Promotion
Article 84 – In implementing paragraph (18) of the general policies of the Seventh Five-Year Plan and in order to achieve the following quantitative goals, action shall be taken in accordance with the provisions of this chapter:
Table No. (19) - Quantitative objectives of performance indicators for domestic policy and social health promotion
Performance measure	One	Quantitative goal at the end of the program
Improving the social capital index	Percentage	۲۰
Crime reduction	Percentage	۵۰
Reducing the prevalence rate of drug use	Percentage	۱۰
Increasing the number of recovered addicts	Percentage	۵
Increasing the empowerment of socially disadvantaged women	Percentage	۵۰
The Ministry of Interior is required to submit an annual report to the Parliament on the performance indicators of domestic policy and social health promotion.
Article 85 – In order to promote social health and prevent, monitor and reduce social problems and harms, and observe social discipline, the following measures shall be taken by the relevant executive bodies within the framework of the approvals of the Social Council of the country and in compliance with the approvals of the Supreme Council of the Cultural Revolution:
A- The Ministry of Interior, through the relevant subordinate organization and the Secretariat of the National Social Council, is responsible for compiling and monitoring the country's social status indicators, coordinating and integrating the relevant agencies, and following up and supervising their programs and actions. The Secretary of the National Social Council is appointed by the Minister of Interior.
The relevant executive bodies are required to formulate their extraordinary programs in the field of monitoring and reducing social harms such as divorce, addiction, marginalization, corruption, and lack of social discipline in cooperation with the relevant subordinate organization and submit them to the approval of the National Social Council by the end of July of each year with the approval of the organization. The organization is required to provide the necessary funds for the implementation of extraordinary programs for monitoring and reducing social harms based on valid indicators and appropriate timing in the annual budget bills of the country.
Note: The Ministry of Interior is required to prepare the statute of the country's social affairs organization and submit it to the Council of Ministers for approval within a maximum of six months from the date of entry into force of this law.
B- Primary prevention of social harms through improving the level of knowledge and life skills, reducing risk factors, and strengthening protective factors, with an emphasis on an integrated prevention system with priority given to student, academic, and labor sectors.
C- In line with policy-making and timely action in the field of preventing social issues and harms, the Ministry of Interior, through the relevant subordinate organization, is required to compile a national report on the country's social situation annually and make it available to relevant agencies and institutions, and send a copy of the report to the Parliament.
D- Developing and improving the structure of social emergency centers with the aim of providing timely services to people at risk of harm and the socially vulnerable within the framework of relevant laws and regulations.
Note - The government is required to take steps by the end of the second year of the program to provide specialized human resources and equip social emergency centers with priority for vehicles in cities with more than fifty thousand people.
E- In order to identify and organize vulnerable and crisis-causing social points in urban areas, city outskirts, and informal settlements, the following measures will be taken, centered on the Ministry of Interior through the relevant subordinate organization, and with maximum use of the capacity of jihadi groups, middle circles, and residents through legal local popular development and progress institutions, in coordination with the Basij Mostazafin Organization, and in compliance with the laws in these areas:
1- Identify the physical, demographic, economic, social, and cultural components of the residents of these areas and record relevant information in the social damage management system in compliance with the National Data and Information Management Law by the end of the second year of the program.
2- Reducing factors of social exclusion and deprivation, empowering socially disadvantaged groups and strata, and improving the quality of life of residents in these areas while observing Islamic standards.
Note: The Ministry of Interior is required to take legal action regarding the organization of non-governmental organizations as well as local grassroots development and progress institutions in order to empower neighborhoods, eliminate poverty and deprivation, reduce social harm, promote production and employment, and improve livelihoods, anticipate or create necessary arrangements, provide moral support, material assistance, technical and credit assistance, and provide facilities and amenities.
3- Strengthening solidarity, participation, and a sense of belonging among residents through the determination and implementation of collective socio-cultural programs.
Note - In line with popularization and optimal use of government facilities and the role of the people in solving crises, damages and challenges in critical and vulnerable neighborhoods, the regulations on the integrated intervention of executive agencies, public non-governmental institutions and organizations, and the National Welfare Organization in neighborhoods and outskirts of cities, using the capacity of the intermediate circles, will be prepared by the Ministry of Interior and in cooperation with the Qubr Baqiyatullah Headquarters and will be approved by the Council of Ministers.
C- Preventing the development of marginalization with the approach of enhancing the quality of life of residents of immigrant-sending centers (reverse migration) through an integrated and appropriate distribution of resources and facilities commensurate with the deprivation index by the organization and in cooperation with the Ministry of Interior, municipalities, the Judiciary, the Ministry of Roads and Urban Development, the Islamic Revolution Housing Foundation, the Mostazafan Foundation, the Executive Headquarters of the Imam's Decree (RA), and the Basij Sazandegi Organization within the framework of relevant documents and regulations and approvals of the Supreme Council for Land Planning.
G- In order to promote social health and security of the country against the threat of drugs, psychotropic substances and addiction, the following measures will be taken within the framework of general anti-drug policies and the Anti-Drug Law approved on 3/8/1998 with subsequent amendments and additions:
1- The Anti-Drug Headquarters is required, in cooperation with the Ministries of Education, Science, Research and Technology, Health, Medical Treatment and Education, Cooperatives, Labor and Social Welfare, Culture and Islamic Guidance, Sports and Youth, the Islamic Republic of Iran Broadcasting Organization, Islamic Azad University, and other non-governmental educational institutions and centers, to implement addiction prevention programs and activities using scientific methods and modern technologies in educational, work, family, and urban and rural environments, with priority given to the country's student population, with the aim of reducing the prevalence of addiction by ten percent (10%) at the end of the program compared to the first year of the action plan, and to submit a report on the measures taken, broken down by implementing agencies, to the country's social and internal affairs commissions and the councils of the parliament every six months.
2- The Anti-Drug Headquarters is required to cooperate with legally competent agencies, including the National Welfare Organization, the National Prisons and Security and Educational Measures Organization, and the Ministry of Health, Treatment and Medical Education, in compliance with the laws, utilizing the capacity of non-governmental organizations and the private sector, and implementing scientific programs and standard and effective activities in the field of treatment, rehabilitation, and harm reduction for addicts, to expand the quantity and quality of treatment centers, reduce harm, and improve services in such a way that the number of recovered addicts increases by one percent (1%) annually compared to the year the program began. The aforementioned headquarters is required to send a report on the measures taken, broken down by implementing agencies, to the Social Affairs, Internal Affairs, Councils, and Health and Treatment Commissions of the Parliament every six months.
۳–
1-3- The Anti-Narcotics Headquarters is required to take action through the competent legal authorities in order to undermine the financial and economic foundations of traffickers, pursue the discovery and identification of the traffickers' movable and immovable property and the networks for the production, distribution and transportation of narcotics, psychotropic substances and precursors (especially drug lords and network leaders) inside and outside the country.
2-3- The judiciary is required to take action to reduce the delay in proceedings and the criminal population in determining the fate of related cases and issuing final verdicts in the shortest possible time.
3-3- Fines related to the Anti-Drug Law and its subsequent amendments and additions, after the treasury circulates in the form of an annual budget, based on the approval of the Headquarters, in accordance with the laws and by exchanging agreements between the organization and the relevant executive agencies, are made available to the relevant executive agencies.
4- The Ministry of Interior, in cooperation with the General Staff of the Armed Forces, is required to take steps, within the limits of legally approved resources, to create sustainable security in border areas and prevent smuggling, supply and transit of narcotics and psychotropic substances into the country, through the intelligentization, blocking and hardware and software monitoring (control) of the country's land, air and sea borders, especially the eastern borders, in such a way that the annual rate of narcotics and psychotropic substances discoveries in the eastern and eastern peripheral regions of the country increases by at least five percent (5%) compared to the base year (1401).
5- The Anti-Narcotics Headquarters is required to conduct regular annual addiction epidemiological studies in order to formulate policies and take accurate, objective, and timely measures in the field of prevention, treatment, and rehabilitation of addicts.
H- In order to identify and prevent smuggling of goods and currency and complete the information of the system for identifying and combating smuggling of goods and currency, subject to Note (3) of Article (5) of the Law on Combating Smuggling of Goods and Currency, the Judiciary and the National Real Estate Registration Organization are required, within a maximum of six months from the entry into force of this law, in compliance with the National Data and Information Management Law, in addition to online information exchange, to provide the possibility of online inquiry of all records of definitive convictions, as well as information on smuggling suspects and the incarceration of convicted smugglers in civil and criminal courts, as well as all registered and judicial executions, stating the subject of the case and the type and amount of the conviction, information on the execution of the sentences of these cases, including the amount of the conviction paid and unpaid, the status of the incarceration and related sentences, criminal security orders and security requests issued, and properties seized in the execution of the security, all information on the seizure of properties and documents of smuggling suspects and convicted smugglers in judicial courts and registration enforcement departments, and the status of the fulfillment of obligations of persons in registration enforcement departments, in a structured and exploitable manner, through the National Information Exchange Center for the aforementioned system.
The executive regulations of this paragraph shall be prepared by the Judiciary's Center for Statistics and Information Technology in cooperation with the Ministry of Communications and Information Technology and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
X- The Headquarters for Combating Smuggling of Goods and Currency is required to announce, within three months of the entry into force of this law, a comprehensive five-year plan for combating smuggling of goods and currency, with the aim of reducing smuggling of goods by at least fifteen percent (15%) annually, by separate executive agencies. This headquarters is required to publish a periodic report on the performance of the executive agencies in implementing the said plan to the public every six months.
D- The Judiciary is required to plan and prepare the groundwork for reducing crime and misdemeanors with the aim of reducing it by ten percent (10%) annually, especially in important instances, through the relevant agencies, and in addition to public announcement, to monitor its implementation and submit annual performance reports of the agencies to the Parliament.
Z- In order to prevent crimes related to mobile phone SIM cards or equivalent telecommunications IDs, the Ministry of Communications and Information Technology is obliged to unilaterally or block, directly or upon notification by the judiciary, the SIM cards of deceased persons, liquidated or closed legal entities, non-Iranian citizens with temporary residence who have left the country, and prisoners during their stay in prison, except in cases ordered by the judicial authority, until the legal owner determines the responsibility, as the case may be. Authorities holding information subject to this paragraph are obliged to provide the necessary information to the Ministry of Communications and Information Technology.
R- In order to develop cooperation between municipalities and rural municipalities in the country, establish contacts with international unions of municipalities, transfer experiences, organize and implement training programs, examine the issues and problems of municipalities, provide appropriate solutions and suggestions, and increase the communication of municipalities with the three branches of government and follow up on related matters, the Union of Municipalities of the Country with the membership of all municipalities in the country will be established in the form of a non-governmental organization by obtaining a license from the Ministry of Interior without imposing any financial burden on the government.
The Ministry of Interior is required to submit a report on the performance of this section to the Internal Affairs Commission and the Majlis Councils every six months.
G- A comprehensive human resources management system for municipalities (except Tehran Municipality) commensurate with the duties and powers of the municipality in the areas of recruitment, employment, management training and development, employee performance evaluation, municipal performance evaluation, promotion and appointment, termination of service, insurance and social security, welfare and health affairs, and the system of salaries and benefits for municipal employees shall be prepared by the Ministry of Interior within three months of the entry into force of this law and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers in accordance with the laws and regulations. The Ministry of Interior is required to submit an annual report on the performance of this section to the Internal Affairs Commission and the Councils of the Parliament.
G- The chairman or elected member of the Supreme Council of Provinces will be added as an observer member to the composition of the Supreme Council of Urban Planning and Architecture of Iran, the Social Council of the Country, the Supreme Council of Cultural Heritage, Tourism and Handicrafts, the Supreme Council for Environmental Protection, and the Supreme Council for Transportation and Safety Coordination of the Country.
Article 86 – In order to organize immigrants and foreign nationals, the Ministry of Interior, in cooperation with the Secretariat of the Supreme National Security Council, is required to:
A- Establish a national migration organization.
Note - The structure, duties, and powers of the aforementioned organization shall be approved by the Parliament.
B- In cooperation with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Intelligence, the Intelligence Organization of the Islamic Revolutionary Guard Corps, the Statistical Center of Iran, the Police Command of the Islamic Republic of Iran, the National Civil Registration Organization, and other executive agencies, take action to organize, enter, exit, expel, census, territorial planning, and register foreign nationals, asylum seekers, and legal and illegal immigrants in a way that all information on immigrants and foreign nationals is collected in an online and integrated reference database, and its exploitation portals are created for other agencies based on Article (7) of the National Data and Information Management Law.
Note - The provision of any services to foreign nationals other than in emergency situations, such as the need for treatment in cases of life-threatening situations, as well as in cases related to reputational and life-threatening situations in criminal, law enforcement, and judicial matters, by executive agencies must be based on the identity information of this system.
Chapter 19 – Improving the Education System
Article 87 – In implementing paragraph (20) of the general policies of the Seventh Five-Year Plan and in order to achieve the following quantitative goals, action shall be taken in accordance with the provisions of this chapter:
Table No. (20) - Quantitative objectives of performance indicators for improving the education system
Performance measure	One	Quantitative goal at the end of the program
Ratio of student teachers to full-time (face-to-face) faculty at Shahid Rajaee Universities of Education and Teacher Training	Person	۳۰
Ratio of full-time faculty of assistant professor and above to total faculty members in Shahid Rajaee Universities of Education and Teacher Training	Percentage	۸۰
Per capita educational and educational space in schools	Square meter	۶.۱
Per capita indoor sports space	Square meter	۱
Student to Educational Instructor Ratio (National Average)	Person	۱۵۰
Schools without a developmental teacher with a population of more than (75) students	Number	۰
Student-to-Physical Education Teacher Ratio	Person	۲۸۰
Smart and technology-based classrooms (with priority given to disadvantaged areas)	Percentage	۵۰
