Human capital
Article 88 – In order to improve the quality of the education and training human resources as the axis of change in the country's education and training system, the following measures shall be taken:
A- The Ministry of Education is required to prepare a “Comprehensive Document on Human Capital in Education, Including Recruitment, Selection, Training, Employment, Retention, Promotion, Retirement, and Termination of Service” within three months of the entry into force of this law, based on the upstream documents, including the “General Policies for Creating Transformation in the Country’s Education System” announced by the Supreme Leader and the “Document on Fundamental Transformation of Education” approved by the Supreme Council of the Cultural Revolution and the Law on the Selection of Teachers and Education Staff approved on 14/6/1936, and to implement the necessary legal arrangements for its ratification and implementation.
B- The country's administrative and employment organization and the organization are required to provide the Ministry of Education with the employment ranks and funding required for education and training, and the student recruitment capacity at Shahid Rajaee Universities of Education and Teacher Training to recruit student teachers, during the implementation of the program, until the approval and implementation of the document subject to paragraph "A" of this article.
Recruiting and training the required personnel in educational and training professions is carried out exclusively through Shahid Rajaee Educational and Teacher Training Universities, by strengthening their infrastructure and capacities, and developing them quantitatively and qualitatively, and with the agreement and cooperation of the seminary management centers, based on the instructions prepared by the Qom Seminary Management Center in partnership with the Khorasan and Isfahan Seminary Management Centers (for training and empowering teachers of Islamic studies, the Quran, and educational affairs instructors) and other government and non-government universities.
If the required teachers are not available through the aforementioned universities, the Ministry of Education is authorized to provide its required manpower from among undergraduate and graduate students with general and specialized qualifications from other public and non-public universities or seminaries by completing a skill training course or student teacher training at Shahid Rajaee Universities of Education and Teacher Training, while studying at a public or non-public university or seminary, with the possibility of receiving a grant of fifty percent (50%) of the minimum salary from the time of studying at Shahid Rajaee Universities of Education and Teacher Training.
The regulations for recruiting these students will be prepared by the Ministry of Education within three months of the law coming into effect and will be approved by the Council of Ministers after obtaining the opinion of the Supreme Council of Education.
Students of Shahid Rajaee Universities of Education and Teacher Training are evaluated annually during their studies, and in case of ineligibility due to the discovery of a lack of legal conditions or loss of legal conditions, their employment relationship will be terminated. The Administrative and Employment Organization of the country and the Ministry of Education are required to submit a report on the measures taken to the Education, Research and Technology Commission of the Parliament annually.
Note - The Ministry of Education, in coordination with the National Administrative and Employment Affairs Organization and the organization, took legal action to ensure fairness in payment by the end of the second year of the program regarding the extraordinary allowances for servants and janitors, commensurate with other employees.
C- The Ministry of Education is obliged to take the necessary legal action to establish a special disciplinary system for teachers, in accordance with the approvals of the Supreme Council of the Cultural Revolution. In addition to initial selection, the general, professional, and specialized qualifications of teachers will be assessed during their years of service in the form of a certificate of qualification for the teaching profession and a participatory evaluation system (evaluation by students' families and school administrators) based on the aforementioned disciplinary system, which is consistent with the teacher ranking system.
D- Any recruitment of new personnel through the purchase of educational services, free tuition, and literacy movement teachers, except for those who have been employed in education under these titles for at least one academic year in the past five years, 24 hours a week, in government schools and educational and training centers, is prohibited. The provisions of this decree do not prevent the honorary participation of elites without creating any employment obligation for the government.
E- Employees of the Ministry of Education may become members of the government employees’ savings account at their own discretion. For those employees of the Ministry of Education who have been members of other funds, by changing their membership in the fund, their savings funds will be transferred to the new membership location, separated into the government share, the employee share, and the profit from the investment, for a single time only. Employees of the Ministry of Education who have accepted or will accept membership in any of the funds or employee savings accounts must deposit up to five percent (5%) of their salaries and benefits into their accounts (as applicable in the fund or employee savings account), and the government is also required to fully allocate and pay the equivalent of the contribution of educators to each of the funds or employee savings accounts of which they have accepted membership, in a specific credit line in the annual budget.
Note - The Ministry of Education is required, within a maximum of three months from the entry into force of this law, to take legal action regarding the approval of the statute of the Teachers' Reserve Fund with the aim of determining the legal status and strengthening the financial strength of teachers, resolving their livelihood problems, involving teachers in the board of trustees and management of the fund, creating financial and accounting transparency, and eliminating conflicts of interest. After the approval and entry into force of the statute of the Teachers' Reserve Fund, this fund is required to offer its management shares through the stock market and is not allowed to conduct business. The Ministry of Education is required to submit an annual performance report of this section to the Education, Research, and Technology Commission and the Deputy for Oversight of the Parliament. The government is also required to take legal action regarding the payment of its audited legal debt.
C- If funding is provided in the annual budget laws, the government is authorized to pay the retirement bonus of teachers in the ranks of assistant professor and above at the end of the legally required years for each individual to retire without applying the retirement process, and to agree to their continued service while observing the legal ceiling of retirement requirements.
G- The Ministry of Education is required to employ at least the equivalent number of teachers who leave the service in education through various means, including retirement, buyout, resignation, dismissal, and other cases, in compliance with the statute of Farhangian University, exclusively through this university and Shahid Rajaee Teacher Training University. The organization and the administrative and employment organization of the country are required to issue the required employment license and identification (code).
Educational quality and justice
Article 89 – In order to provide young learners (children under seven years old) and students with quality educational opportunities and to ensure and expand educational justice and teach Islamic values 
and the Islamic Revolution, the Ministry of Education is required to take the following actions in cooperation with relevant agencies by the end of the first year of the program:
A- Design the criteria and regulations for the quality management of kindergartens (taking into account their non-governmental nature), schools, and educational and training centers in the fields of education, training, equipment, and administration, and while informing the managers of the relevant units, obtain the necessary commitments from them for the correct implementation of the announced rules.
B- Determine the credit and per capita student enrollment in accordance with needs, the level of deprivation, and the quality of education and training, and communicate it to each school.
C- Evaluate the performance of schools based on measurable indicators in the educational and training sectors and based on the extent of implementation of the obligations under this article based on the achieved goals.
D- To create a "comprehensive bank of cultural, academic, educational, sports and skills records" for students in the form of an "electronic educational-developmental-training file" in cooperation with relevant agencies, including the National Civil Registration Organization, the Ministries of Health, Medical Education and Communications and Information Technology, and the National Administrative and Employment Organization, in compliance with the National Data and Information Management Law.
E- Redesign and develop technical, vocational, and skills training courses and vocational training in the upper secondary school based on planning and future research and the development of quantitative and qualitative infrastructures of art schools based on support packages approved by the government with the participation of organizations, institutions and public non-governmental institutions, industrial estates, industry owners and businesses, professional unions, guilds and economic enterprises to launch art schools near factories, industrial estates and science and technology parks and art schools affiliated with institutions. The executive regulations of this paragraph shall be prepared with the proposal of the Ministry of Education and Training within a maximum of three months from the entry into force of this law and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
C- In order to enrich the Quranic, cultural, artistic and sports programs in schools and ensure the mental and physical health of students and prevent or deal with social harms and risks of students in a timely and effective manner by utilizing various educational methods and by utilizing the capacity of executive bodies, mosques, holy shrines and seminaries of jihadi groups, organizations of the Mostazafin, Student Mobilization and Educational Mobilization, and the Student Organization of the Islamic Republic of Iran, the Union of Islamic Student Associations, camps of the Ministry of Education, the Center for Intellectual Development of Children and Adolescents, the Student Sports Federation and the participation of talented and interested students and families, based on the "Comprehensive System of Educational Affairs" and the "Social Care System for Students" that will be prepared by the Ministry of Education and in cooperation with the aforementioned bodies and institutions within six months of the entry into force of this law, regarding the facilitation and inclusion of various educational methods, including scientific, cultural, sports, pilgrimage camps, Paths of Light, Jihadist camps and Paths of Student Progress, with due observance of the following considerations: Educational activities shall be carried out from the resources obtained from renting and providing services subject to Article (2) of the Law on the Regulation of Some Financial, Administrative and Support Regulations of the Ministry of Education and other approved funds.
Note 1- It is permissible to use the capacity of schools and education centers, and working and retired teachers and trainers with general, specialized, and professional qualifications, to implement extracurricular programs and research, cultural, and educational activities during non-educational hours and holidays, in compliance with Islamic standards.
Note 2 - In cases where extracurricular educational, skill, cultural, artistic, training and sports services and leisure enrichment are provided for students and families during non-educational hours, the method of providing extracurricular services and utilizing the space and selling the products of government art schools, government schools and government education and training centers, and the method of collecting revenues and spending the funds received from it shall be in accordance with a regulation prepared by the Ministry of Education and approved by the Council of Ministers.
All revenues subject to this clause, after being deposited into the treasury, are allocated in a separate row as income-expenses and one hundred percent (100%) is allocated to the same units.
All services and actions and the manner in which they are provided, the subject of this note, must comply with Sharia standards.
G- The Ministry of Education, through the Center for Intellectual Development of Children and Adolescents, is required to take action, in cooperation with the Ministry of Roads and Urban Development, governorates, municipalities and other executive agencies, in the form of payment of facilities and exploitation of land while maintaining ownership in provincial centers, in order to strengthen faith, education and Islamic ethics, towards the creation of children and adolescents' cities (growth-entertainment), (entertainment-creativity) and (entertainment-skills) by the non-governmental sector. The Center for Intellectual Development of Children and Adolescents is responsible for guiding and supervising the aforementioned cities. The executive regulations of this clause shall be prepared by the Ministry of Education within a maximum of three months from the entry into force of this law and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
H- The Ministry of Education is required to create an in-school sports environment and allocate the human resources, equipment, facilities, and financial resources needed by the Student Sports Federation and its affiliated sports boards and associations, Shahid Rajaee University of Education and Teacher Training, compensate physical education teachers for their services during non-duty hours, and launch educational-health centers and sports talent clubs in the provinces of the country.
X- The Ministry of Education is required to launch a virtual and non-virtual "Youth Entrepreneur" market in order to optimize adolescence, give adolescents an identity, prepare efficient human resources in family and social roles, and target adolescents' leisure time and document adolescents' activities.
D- In the employment exams subject to Article (28) of the Farhangian University Statute, for individuals who have collaborated with governmental and non-governmental units in educational and training matters with the approval of the Ministry of Education, a coefficient of one and one-tenth is calculated for their score obtained in the exam for each year of full-time experience, and this coefficient increases by one-tenth for each additional year of experience, up to a maximum of five years of experience.
Z- Given the urgent need of the Ministry of Education for educational, training and sports spaces for the use of students of various academic courses, all executive agencies and public institutions, with the exception of technical and vocational universities that have been established in spaces belonging to the Ministry of Education and its subsidiaries in previous years, are required to evacuate the aforementioned buildings and spaces and hand them over to the Ministry of Education and Farhangian University by the end of the second year of the program. Otherwise, with the approval of the aforementioned ministry, other property or properties in the same area with a value equivalent to the current appraisal price of those properties must be transferred to the Ministry of Education. If this ruling is not implemented at the beginning of the third year of the program, the organization is required to deduct the current value of the seized properties from the total funds of the occupying agency or institution, other than funds related to necessary and more important costs or those related to claims of non-governmental entities, and add them to the funds of the Ministry of Education (National School Renovation, Development and Equipping Organization and Farhangian University) for the construction and completion of the required educational and training spaces. Any modification or change of use of the property subject to this ruling is prohibited.
The Ministry of Education is required to submit a report on the measures taken under this article, broken down by clause, to the Parliament's Education, Research, and Technology Committee every six months.
Survivors of education
Article 90 - To attract those who have left primary education, the Ministry of Education is required to take the following measures:
A- Developing a "curriculum appropriate for attracting those who have left education" in order to diversify and create flexibility in the implementation of programs, methods, and educational hours, and approving it in the Supreme Council of Education.
B- Providing and providing free textbooks and meals, support packages (such as stationery and bags, shoes and clothing, and travel expenses), and educational resources and educational assistance for the student or providing assistance from support institutions to his family through educational units.
C- Developing boarding schools, central village, nomadic, exceptional schools, and distance education, with priority given to providing transportation costs for rural, nomadic, and exceptional students (especially girls).
The Ministry of Education is required to submit an annual report on the performance of this article to the Parliament's Education, Research, and Technology Committee.
Management system
Article 91-
A- In order to enhance productivity and improve the management systems of education, the Ministry of Education is required to review its administrative structure and organization in accordance with the missions stipulated in the document on the fundamental transformation of education at all levels and the realization of comprehensive education, with emphasis on the following matters by the end of the first year of the program, and submit the reform proposal to the Council of Ministers for approval after approval by the country's administrative and employment organization:
1- Establishing the school model in line with the fundamental transformation document of education, with an emphasis on linking the school with the institution of the mosque, religious, revolutionary, and cultural institutions, the center for the intellectual development of children and adolescents, jihadi groups, and the family, and attracting popular educational and training participation, and granting the necessary financial, managerial, educational, and training authorities to the relevant schools.
2- Strengthening public schools in various quantitative and qualitative aspects in the fields of science, education, skills, and communication with the community and family (school-centered principle)
3- Eliminating unnecessary and parallel structures in the headquarters, provinces, and regions
4- Granting the necessary administrative and financial authorities (contracting) and strengthening the decision-making level to the school's organs in order to realize the school as a neighborhood educational center in order to implement Notes (1) and (2) of Clause "C" of Article (89) of this law.
5- Applying modern technologies in providing administrative and educational services and systemizing services and work processes, with an emphasis on completing and integrating the statistical system and applied education systems in compliance with the National Data and Information Management Law.
6- Creating a suitable platform for the activities of school-aided charities and educational and training endowments, as well as charity centers.
B- The Ministry of Education is required to take the necessary legal action within six months of the entry into force of this law to revise the statute of the Literacy Movement of the Islamic Republic of Iran, approved on 3/3/1933, with the aim of completely eradicating absolute illiteracy and developing and deepening literacy in order to promote general literacy in society based on new concepts and continuous universal education.
Education as a national issue
Article 92 – In order to create a transformation in the education system and emphasize the cooperation of all elements and activists, the following measures will be taken:
A- With reference to Section "D" of Chapter Eight of the Fundamental Transformation of Education Document, executive agencies are required to make their facilities and resources available based on the needs of educational, training and sports units of the Ministry of Education, based on the national division of labor program and the roadmap for implementing the Fundamental Transformation of Education Document, and the monitoring model and system of indicators and evaluation standards of this document, which will be prepared within three months of the entry into force of this law by the Ministry of Education and approved by the county planning working group (committee) and approved by the Council of Ministers.
B- The organization is required to take action to ensure the mental and physical health of students and prevent and deal with social harms and risky behaviors of students in a timely and effective manner, using the legal capacities at its disposal, including the capacities of the organizations and institutions in charge, including the Ministry of Interior, the country's welfare organizations, the Islamic Republic of Iran Broadcasting, the National Social Council, and medical, support, law enforcement, judicial, cultural, sports, and educational institutions, and to pool the resources that can be allocated for this purpose.
C- The organization is required to formulate and implement policies to support school-building donors and to include the equivalent of their realized donations in the annual budget to complete the donors' incomplete plans (projects), provided that the construction site is determined in accordance with approved plans and based on land-use planning documents.
T-
1- In order to demolish, reconstruct, and strengthen schools and universities, and provide educational equipment, the government is required to allocate two-tenths of a percent of the existing value-added tax revenue to education (the National School Development, Renovation, and Equipping Organization) and Farhangian, Shahid Rajaee, and Technical and Vocational Universities.
2- The National Tax Affairs Organization is obliged to consider the costs of all non-governmental natural and legal entities in the construction, development, completion and equipping of educational, research and technological spaces, boarding houses, libraries, sports halls, workshops and art schools, as appropriate, affiliated with the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Science, Research and Technology, the Ministry of Health, Treatment and Medical Education and seminaries, including educational spaces and student dormitories of Shahid Rajaee Universities of Education and Secretary Training, centers for vocational and technical training and assessment of professional skills and qualifications, and cultural centers of the Intellectual Development Center for Children and Adolescents, which are carried out within the framework of the approvals of the Provincial Planning and Development Council, as appropriate, with the approval of the National School Development, Renovation and Equipping Organization, the National Technical and Vocational Education Organization, the Ministry of Science, Research and Technology, the Ministry of Health, Treatment and Medical Education, and the Seminary Management Center, and relevant organizations, as acceptable tax costs.
E- The government is obliged to take the following measures to bring about change in the education system:
1- Implementing the Fundamental Transformation of Education Document in such a way that all actions of the Ministry of Education are carried out based on this document and no action is taken that is contrary to the law and the document.
2- Plan in such a way that the admissions to Shahid Rajaee Educational and Teacher Training Universities will increase by at least twenty-five percent (25%) each year compared to the previous year, up to the ceiling of row (1) of table number (20) of article (87) of this law.
3- In implementing the general policies of Article 44 (44) of the Constitution, any transfer of management and privatization of public schools during the implementation of the program is prohibited.
C- All income, donations and public cash gifts to the Student Organization of the Islamic Republic of Iran, after being deposited into the account of the National Treasury, in the form of a row
Revenue-expenditure is allocated to these units in accordance with paragraph "D" of Article (28) of the Law on the Addition of Certain Articles to the Law on the Regulation of Part of Government Financial Regulations (2). The Ministry of Education is required to spend the deposited amounts in the form of annual budgets only for cultural, educational and sports activities in schools.
G- With the aim of providing and standardizing cooling and heating systems and assisting with educational equipment and teaching aids for schools and art schools in the country, with priority given to deprived areas, the phrase "twenty percent (20%)" in paragraph "b" of Article (65) of the Law on the Addition of Certain Articles to the Law on the Regulation of Part of Government Financial Regulations (2) is amended to "forty percent (40%)".
H- During the implementation of the program, three percent (3%) of the fees referred to in paragraph (3) of Article (13) of the Law on the Establishment of Education Councils in the Provinces, Cities and Regions of the Country, approved on 10/26/1372, with subsequent amendments and additions, will be deposited directly into the account of the Ministry of Education with the General Treasury of the Country through a separate receipt by the individual to be used for the purposes stated in the aforementioned law.
X- Expenses incurred by donors in the construction, completion, and equipping of development projects licensed by the organization or licensed under Article (23) of the Law on the Addition of Certain Articles to the Law on the Regulation of Part of Government Financial Regulations (2) or listed in the tables of the country's annual budget law and provincial plans approved by the provincial planning and development council, upon the proposal of the relevant executive body and with the approval of the organization, are considered acceptable tax expenses.
D- The Ministry of Education is required to use resources from the development of properties, lands, and small-scale or demolished schools, as well as its annual property acquisition budget or other sources, including social contributions and donors, to build at least two hundred large-scale educational and educational complexes (Hayat Tayyiba), with priority given to its own lands or those of affiliated agencies. The Ministry of Roads and Urban Development is also required to anticipate and allocate the lands required for the aforementioned project in the urban layout.
Note - A large-scale educational and training complex (Hayat Tayyiba) refers to a collection of educational and training units that have different academic courses with at least 36 classes and 1,000 students, in a full-scale area including educational, training, laboratory, workshop and sports spaces.
Chapter 20 – Improving the scientific, technological and research system
Article 93 – In implementing paragraph (20) of the general policies of the Seventh Five-Year Plan and in order to achieve the following quantitative goals, actions will be taken in accordance with the provisions of this chapter, in compliance with Islamic principles and the approvals of the Supreme Council of the Cultural Revolution:
Table No. (21) - Quantitative objectives of performance indicators for improving the scientific, technological and research system
