The Ministry of Justice is required to submit a report on the performance indicators of judicial and legal development to the Parliament annually.
Article 113 – In order to facilitate the handling of legal cases and resolve people’s disputes, the Judiciary and the Ministry of Justice, in compliance with the National Data and Information Management Law, are required to take the following measures as appropriate:
A- By the end of the second year of the program, they should enable the performance of tasks such as case referral, scheduling, and expert selection using modern technologies, including artificial intelligence, to assist the judge while maintaining the judge's personal responsibility. The executive regulations for this section will be prepared within the framework of the policies announced by the Supreme Cyberspace Council and will be approved by the Head of the Judiciary.
B- By the end of the program, legal files will be electronic and replace paper files.
C- Create the possibility of online and immediate inquiry through the Judiciary's smart financial inquiry system (SAHQ) regarding the financial status of claimants of insolvency or bankruptcy, convicted persons and debtors in the enforcement departments and registration enforcement departments, and if necessary, provide the competent judicial authority and registration enforcement departments with the possibility of seizing convicted persons and debtors in registration enforcement files. In the event of inquiry, if the executive agencies have information about the assets of individuals, they are obliged to provide the aforementioned information to the Judiciary online in the implementation of this ruling.
D- Launch the "Transparency of the Performance of Lawyers and Official Experts" system for lawyers of the Bar Association, lawyers and experts of the Bar Center, official experts and family advisors of the Judiciary, and experts of the Association of Official Experts of the Judiciary by the end of the first year of the program. In addition to foreseeing the possibility of complaining about a lawyer or expert and the possibility of announcing and reporting their violations, as well as foreseeing a process for obtaining the opinions of clients and stakeholders at the end of each case, they should make available to the public performance information exclusively including the number of cases and their subjects without including the confidential content of the cases, the rate of attendance at court sessions, and the payment of taxes and government fees. If the number of reported violations in a case exceeds five, the prosecutor of the relevant association or center, as the public prosecutor, is obliged to directly take action and follow up on the matter until a final verdict is issued, if there is sufficient evidence and evidence.
E- The National Civil Registration Organization is required to issue and notify the heirs and beneficiaries of the inheritance monopoly certificate referred to in Article (360) of the Civil Affairs Law approved on 2/4/1319, in compliance with Article 12 (12) of the Constitution of the Islamic Republic of Iran and the Law on Permission to Observe the Personal Status of Non-Shiite Iranians in Courts approved on 31/4/1312, based on existing data and information, such as the causal and relative database, and without the need for a request from the heirs and beneficiaries, within twenty days after the registration of the death event. The aforementioned inheritance monopoly certificate may be appealed within ten days after notification to the Dispute Resolution Board referred to in Article (3) of the Civil Registration Law approved on 16/4/1355, and the decision of the aforementioned board may be appealed within twenty days in a competent court. This ruling does not prevent the filing of a lawsuit to prove lineage and enforce a will, and the like, before the courts.
The National Records and Property Registration Organization is required to send a copy of the official will to the National Civil Registration Organization after registering the signature.
The State Registration Organization is required to immediately and instantly announce the certificate of exclusive inheritance to the State Documents and Real Estate Registration Organization, the Islamic Republic of Iran Police Command, the State Taxation Organization, the Securities and Exchange Organization, the Central Bank, and other executive agencies of the applicant after issuance. The State Registration Organization is required to immediately register the certificate of exclusive inheritance in the Comprehensive Documents and Real Estate System after receipt and reflect it in subsequent inquiries.
The executive regulations of this clause shall be prepared by the Ministry of Justice in cooperation with the National Civil Registration Organization within a maximum period of three months from the date of entry into force of this law, and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers after approval by the Chief of the Judiciary.
C- The Judiciary is required to take legal action regarding the following matters by the end of the first year of the program to organize power of attorneys and peace agreements:
1- Providing proposed sample contract texts for use by the parties to the contract based on their consent or non-consent in each case, including the subject matter, type of contract, obligations and contractual conditions in notary offices and classifying them with priority given to power of attorney or peace agreements regarding immovable property, automobiles and company shares.
2- Creating a comprehensive database of power of attorneys and peace agreements based on a unique identifier and with the ability to query according to the laws
G- To utilize the capacities of the people and develop participatory and non-judicial methods in resolving disputes without imposing any financial burden from the public and private resources at their disposal, and without developing the organization:
1- In order to develop alternative methods of judicial proceedings such as arbitration, mediation, peace and reconciliation, and negotiation, the Judiciary, through the Dispute Resolution Center, has taken the necessary legal measures.
2- In order to develop public participation and receive donations, grants, income from endowments and cash gifts from individuals and legal entities, the Judiciary, through the Dispute Resolution Center, shall make the necessary arrangements to open a “Peace Charity Account” with the National Treasury under the name “Judiciary Dispute Resolution Center – National Patience Headquarters” by the end of the first year of the implementation of this law. The funds obtained, in accordance with the instructions approved by the Head of the Judiciary, shall be spent exclusively for the same purposes as those intended by the donors after the treasury has been circulated.
H- In the first year of the program’s implementation, the government is required to increase the judiciary’s share of the country’s general revenues by thirty percent (30%) compared to the base year 1402, in addition to the annual increase, and this increase will be considered as the base figure for the judiciary’s budget in subsequent years of the program.
X- In order to facilitate people's access to judicial services, such as submitting and following up on petitions or complaints electronically, the Judiciary is required to create an automated system for all individuals by the end of the first year of the program so that all required requests can be sent offline and through the judicial services portal.
D- In order to expedite the handling of traffic accidents resulting in unintentional bodily injuries, with the exception of cases subject to Articles (714) and (715) of Book Five of the Islamic Penal Code (Penalties and Deterrent Punishments), the Police Command of the Islamic Republic of Iran is obliged to determine the cause of the accident directly or through an accident expert and introduce the injured person to the forensic medicine. The accident expert report and the forensic medicine report, as the case may be, are notified by the Police Command of the Islamic Republic of Iran and the Forensic Medicine Organization of the country through the Electronic Judicial Notification System (SANA) to the parties and the insurance company or the Physical Damage Fund. The judiciary is obliged to provide the possibility of notifying the subject of this ruling through the Electronic Judicial Notification System (SANA). If the aforementioned opinions are not objected to within a period of one week after notification, the insurer or the fund is obliged to pay the physical damages to the injured person without the need for a court decision and within a maximum of twenty days after the end of the objection period, in accordance with the forensic medicine theory, whether initial or final. In case of objection, the matter will be registered by the Islamic Republic of Iran Police Command and the file, along with the plaintiff's complaint, will be referred to the judicial authority for consideration.
Note 1- Regarding the issue of Articles (714) and (715) of Book Five of the Islamic Penal Code (Penalties and Deterrent Punishments) and other cases where the case is examined by a judicial authority after an objection, if the parties, the insurer or the fund, as the case may be, do not object to the aforementioned opinions or waive their objection, the insurer or the fund is obliged to take action to pay the physical damages in accordance with the forensic medical opinion, whether initial or final, without the need to issue a court ruling and upon notification by the judicial authority within a maximum of twenty days.
Note 2 - The ruling of this paragraph, which denies the prosecution of the general aspect of the crimes mentioned in Articles (716) and (717) of Book Five of the Islamic Penal Code (Penalties and Deterrent Punishments), is not in accordance with the relevant laws.
The executive regulations of this paragraph shall be prepared by the Ministry of Justice, in cooperation with relevant authorities, within a maximum period of three months from the entry into force of this law, and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers after approval by the Chief of the Judiciary.
Z- In important cases, the judiciary is obliged, at its discretion, to take the necessary legal measures in cooperation with the Ministries of Justice and Foreign Affairs in investigating crimes against human rights, including genocide, crimes against humanity, terrorism, war crimes, and aggression in other countries by natural or legal persons or governments, especially crimes committed by Western governments, and to submit their reports to the competent domestic and international authorities.
R- Referral to arbitration regarding government and public immovable properties and the enforcement of awards issued by arbitration authorities regarding all immovable properties, as the case may be, is subject to compliance with Article 139 (139) of the Constitution, Paragraph (5) of Article (489) of the Code of Procedure of Public and Revolutionary Courts (in Civil Matters) approved on 21/1/1379, and inquiry into ownership from the National Real Estate and Documents Registration Organization and the Ministry of Economic Affairs and Finance, otherwise the arbitration award is invalid.
G- In implementing Article 49 (49) of the Constitution, the government is required to notify the relevant authorities of information and documents regarding the illicit assets covered by this Article, pursue the matter until a final conclusion is reached, and take the necessary steps to return the assets resulting from corruption that have left the country through competent international authorities.
Article 114 – In order to protect the rights of the people in implementing registration and facilitating people’s access to registration services, the National Real Estate and Documents Registration Organization is required to do the following, in compliance with the National Data and Information Management Law:
A- By the end of the first year of the program, launch the "Automated System for the Execution of the Provisions of Official Enforceable Documents" with capabilities such as the ability to register all requests required in the execution process offline and without human intervention, calling up information and data necessary for issuing electronic execution from authorities with information related to enforceable documents, viewing all information and documents related to the execution case for the parties to the case, and online and instant arrest and release of arrest of all properties with a cadastral document with an electronic property office number, while respecting the principle of confidentiality for courts of justice, registration enforcement departments, and other legally licensed authorities.
Note: All executive agencies and all authorities holding the information and data necessary for issuing electronic executive orders are required to provide the aforementioned information online and instantly after inquiring about the system subject to this paragraph.
B- Amend the comprehensive property and documents system in such a way that it is possible to register all rights related to real estate, such as ownership of real property, ownership of benefits, usufruct, easement, mortgage rights, goodwill, business and trade rights, as well as the possibility of online and real-time registration of legal acts (such as obligations and contracts), legal events, final decisions and judicial orders regarding these properties, as well as the possibility of online and real-time responses to inquiries made regarding the information contained in this system. The judiciary is obliged to provide the judicial decisions and orders subject to this paragraph to the National Property and Documents Registration Organization online and real-time for registration in the aforementioned system.
Note - After the end of the first year of the program, if the executive agencies subject to the Law on Facilitating the Preparation of Official Documents approved on 24/5/1385 have the right to receive claims based on the response to the inquiry, they are required to immediately notify the National Document and Property Registration Organization and the inquirer's office online after the inquiry. Otherwise, the notary is required to prepare and register the document without collecting the claims, and the registration office, notary, and transferee will not have any responsibility or obligation regarding the uncollected claims. This does not prevent them from referring to the transferor or the debt creator, as the case may be.
The organization is required to provide, in cooperation with relevant executive agencies, the possibility of paying the claims subject to this clause through the electronic document registration system and in the registry.
C- In order to facilitate the provision of registration services and accelerate the implementation of the comprehensive law
The National Cadastre, approved on 12/11/1393, shall take legal action regarding the issuance of technical, engineering, and legal brokerage licenses for qualified legal entities.
D- In implementing the National Data and Information Management Law and in order to prevent crimes and promote the safety of motor vehicle transactions, the Ministry of Communications and Information Technology is required, in cooperation with institutions and organizations that have information about motor vehicles, including the Islamic Republic of Iran Police Command, the Judiciary's Center for Statistics and Information Technology, and the National Real Estate and Documents Registration Organization, to provide private sector platforms with the possibility of online inquiry of information and records related to the properties being traded, as well as the trading qualifications and competence of individuals, subject to the consent of the parties to the transaction, while observing confidentiality and privacy considerations. In this regard, the Islamic Republic of Iran Police Command is required to provide the possibility of registering motor vehicle transactions before changing the license plate through the aforementioned platforms.
The executive regulations of this clause shall be prepared by the Ministry of Communications and Information Technology and the Ministry of Industry, Mines and Trade in cooperation with the aforementioned agencies and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
Article 115 – In order to reduce the delay in proceedings and improve forensic medicine services, the following measures shall be taken:
A- The Forensic Medicine Organization of the country is required to establish an electronic system for providing forensic medicine services, including examinations, laboratories, dissection, and commissions, by the end of the first year of the program, in compliance with the National Data and Information Management Law, and to send answers to all inquiries from judicial agencies and authorities and the Islamic Republic of Iran’s Law Enforcement Command online and instantly. The Ministry of Health, Medical Education, Social Security Organization, Law Enforcement Command of the Islamic Republic of Iran, and judicial authorities are required to provide medical documents, correspondence, and reports to the Forensic Medicine Organization of the country online and instantly.
B- The Forensic Medicine Organization of the country is authorized, in compliance with Islamic principles, to take the necessary legal measures to assign the forensic medicine services required by executive bodies, public non-governmental institutions and organizations, diagnostic and treatment centers, insurance companies, the public, and some of the duties of Article (1) of the Law on the Establishment of the Forensic Medicine Organization of the Country, approved on 27/4/1372, with the exception of the cases of paragraph (1) of that article, by exercising full supervision over the trusted medical group, which will be appointed for this purpose from among government employees or trustworthy and trustworthy individuals.
The executive regulations of this paragraph shall be prepared by the Forensic Medicine Organization of the country in cooperation with the Ministries of Justice and Health, Treatment and Medical Education, and shall be approved by the Chief Justice.
C- The country's forensic medicine organization is authorized to recruit doctors on general duty after the end of their term of service and specialist doctors subject to service, a plan, a coefficient (K), and assistance based on satisfaction with their performance after obtaining legal permits from the country's administrative and employment organization within the approved budget, on a competitive basis and in compliance with service regulations, with priority for recruitment in deprived and remote areas.
D- The Ministry of Health, Treatment and Medical Education should create the necessary capacity in the national exam to train doctors to serve in the country's forensic medicine, with priority given to recruiting in deprived and remote areas.
Article 116–
A- During the years of implementation of this law, prisoners who, while incarcerated, have managed to memorize the entire Holy Quran and Nahjul-Balagha, obtain a master's degree or higher, or actively participate in cultural activities, will be given priority in being offered pardon and sentence reduction.
B- In implementing general judicial policies and principles one hundred and fifty-seven (157), one hundred and fifty-eight (158) and one hundred and sixty (160) of the Constitution, the responsibility, duties and executive (administrative and financial) powers of the Judiciary, using internal resources and within the ceiling of approved funds (with due regard to Article fifty-three (53) of the Constitution) and observing the rules of this chapter and other rules and regulations, shall be the responsibility of the Head of the Judiciary.
C- With the approach of fairness in payments and coordination between job groups within the approved budget ceiling, the guideline subject to Note Article (7) of the Law on Administrative and Employment Regulations of the General Inspectorate of the Country, approved on 11/2/1363, will be prepared by that organization within six months and will be approved by the Chief of the Judiciary.
D- In order to optimally protect public resources and government and public rights and properties, an extraordinary specialized legal position or judicial support and incentives, the amount and privileges of which are commensurate with the protection, preservation, optimization, efficiency, and provision of the aforementioned resources, rights, and properties, shall be determined. Its guidelines shall be prepared by the Legal Assistant of the President in cooperation with the Ministry of Justice, the Administrative and Employment Organization of the country, and the organization, and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers.
Article 117 – In order to organize the legal affairs of executive bodies, the following measures shall be taken:
A- The Legal Assistant to the President is required, in cooperation with the Judiciary, the Administrative and Employment Organization of the country, and relevant agencies, to take the necessary measures within six months from the date of entry into force of this law to organize "special administrative authorities" based on observing the principles of fair trial, ensuring people's rights, transparent proceedings, registering complaints, and communicating votes through the creation of a comprehensive, automated, and free online system in compliance with the National Data and Information Management Law, and to include a legal expert from the employees of the executive agencies in all special administrative authorities that handle disputes and violations, with the exception of those in which a judge is a member.
B- Disputes between executive agencies subject to Article (5) of the Civil Service Management Law that are under the executive branch shall be resolved in accordance with Article 134 of the Constitution. If the executive agencies refuse to implement the decision for any reason, the organization shall deduct the amount of the decision from the annual budget appropriations of the relevant agency for the next year and add it to the appropriations of the beneficiary executive agency in accordance with the aforementioned decision. In the case of those state-owned companies or government-affiliated for-profit institutions or non-governmental public institutions and bodies or banks (that do not have a line item in the annual budget or do not have centralized accounts), the implementation of the aforementioned decision from the accounts belonging to them shall be the responsibility of the General Treasury or the Central Bank from the budget appropriations of the following year. In any case, the referral of disputes between executive agencies to the judiciary shall be subject to the approval of the Council of Ministers. The Legal Office of the President shall follow up on the implementation of the decisions taken. Criminal lawsuits are excluded from the provisions of this paragraph.
C- In cases where the opinions of judicial authorities regarding rights and property belonging to the government are subject to the ruling stipulated in Article (477) of the Criminal Procedure Code approved on 4/12/1392, the Vice President for Legal Affairs can report the matter to the relevant authorities.
Program governance structure
Article 118–
A- In order to ensure the proper implementation of the law and to coordinate the activities of the executive bodies, the "High Council for the Management of the Program" is formed under the responsibility of the First Vice President and consists of the head of the organization (secretary of the council), the Minister of Economic Affairs and Finance, and ministers who are the heads of the permanent commissions of the government, and the head of the Program, Budget and Accounts Commission of the Parliament (as an observer). The secretariat of the High Council for the Management of the Program is the responsibility of the organization.
The meetings of the Supreme Council for the Management of the Program are held at least once a month and with the presence of two-thirds of the members, and its decisions are valid by an absolute majority vote of those present after the approval of the President. This council is required to continuously review the performance of the agencies in implementing the program tasks and adopt policies commensurate with the strengths and weaknesses of these measures within the framework of the laws. Within a maximum of two months after the implementation of the law, for each of the main and policy-making agencies with responsibilities in the program that use the public budget, introduce a financial supervisor, at the proposal of the Minister of Economic Affairs and Finance from among the employees or persons with trust and confidence, and an executive supervisor, at the proposal of the head of the organization from among the employees or persons with trust and confidence (after approval at the meeting of the Supreme Council for the Management of the Program), to the relevant agency. The aforementioned agencies are required to provide information and full cooperation within the framework of the tasks assigned to each of the supervisors, within the limits of their legal powers, and the highest official of each agency is responsible for supervising the proper implementation of this matter. Each financial and executive supervisor is required to submit a report to the Secretariat of the Program's Supreme Steering Council every six months, within the scope of his or her mission, on the performance of the executive body in fulfilling the program's tasks and the obstacles facing the failure to fulfill these tasks.
Note 1- The location of each observer will be determined after obtaining approval from the Supreme Council of the Program's Steering Committee, and their term of office is one year, non-renewable, and consistent with the years of program implementation.
Note 2- The responsibility for the accuracy of the semi-annual reports lies with the supervisor, and any false report, as the case may be, is considered a violation or crime and can be investigated by the competent authorities. The Supreme Council for the Management of the Program is required to submit to the Parliament in Shahrivar each year a report on the implementation of this law, including the performance of the previous year and the plan for the next year, and the supporting document for the budget and financing of this law, broken down by executive agencies and chapters of the program, in a quantitative and comparative manner, and the progress of the performance indicators in the tables of this law. After the said report is announced, it is immediately referred to the relevant commission or commissions and the Deputy of the Parliament’s Oversight for review in accordance with the arrangements set forth in Article (141) of the Law on the Internal Regulations of the Islamic Consultative Assembly, in proportion to the chapters of the report. The main commissions are required to review the report and submit their report to the Program, Budget, and Accounting Commission within twenty days after receiving the report. The Program, Budget, and Accounting Commission and the Deputy of the Parliament’s Oversight Commission are required to submit a report on the government’s performance, broken down by responsible agencies, before reviewing the budget bill for the next year in public.
B- The government is obliged to mobilize and utilize all government, non-government, private and cooperative resources and facilities, as well as other domestic and foreign facilities and capacities and public resources, to fully and accurately implement the provisions of the program. The government is obliged to submit to the parliament, within a maximum of six months from the entry into force of this law, its five-year financing plan, divided into program years, after approval by the Supreme Steering Council of the program subject to paragraph "A" of this article.
The table of resources provided for in this paragraph shall be included in the annual budget under the title "Resources for the Implementation of Program Provisions" each year, and the extent of its realization shall be reported in the annual report referred to in Note (2) of Paragraph "A" of this Article.
Article 119 – The government is required to take the necessary action within the framework of the laws regarding the following matters within a maximum of one year after this law comes into force, with an emphasis on establishing a leading institution in accordance with the opinion of the Supreme Board of Supervision over the proper implementation of the general policies of the system and determining the task of improving the administration and management of free commercial-industrial and special economic zones:
1- Developing a quantitative table and methods for mobilizing financial resources to achieve eight percent (8%) economic growth
2- Program to address macroeconomic imbalances
3- Determining the contribution of the private and cooperative sectors in economic growth
4- Requirements for growth of more than twenty-five percent in non-oil exports
5- Growth plan for gross fixed capital formation and trade balance
6- Program to strengthen the share and requirements of leading the knowledge-based economy and increase the share of exports of high-tech products and services
7- Program to improve social justice indicators
8- A program for fair distribution of factors in the production-to-consumption chain, in proportion to their role in creating value, especially in the distribution stage.
9- Program to eliminate unfair discrimination in the use of public resources
10- Tax Justice Realization Program
11- Microfinance System Program
12- Program to strengthen equal and fair opportunities in employment and positions, including managerial, economic, and financial.
13- Non-oil trade imbalance reduction program
14- Capital Account Imbalance Reduction Program
15– Rial Governance and Management Strengthening Program
16- Program to reduce speculation in the foreign exchange market and manage expectations
17- Plan to settle government debts to the Social Security Organization, municipalities, Khatam al-Anbiya Construction Headquarters, and similar cases
18– Program to clarify the revenues and expenses of the National Oil Company
19- Comprehensive program for the penetration of the four technologies: "Information and Communications", "Biotechnology", "Microtechnology", and "New and Renewable Energies"
20- Completion of all program tables, including the current status, the status of each year (separately), and the status at the end of five years.
21- Formulating a plan to implement general policies for sea-based development and increasing the country's share in transit maritime transport and strengthening the combined transport network.
22- Developing a comprehensive document on the progress and development of non-formal and technical and vocational training based on land planning, labor market demand, changes in new technologies, and future jobs.
23- Carrying out the following activities based on the provision of resources in compliance with the approvals of the Supreme Council of the Cultural Revolution and the Council for the Development and Promotion of Humanities and the cooperation of relevant agencies, especially the Ministries of Science, Research and Technology, Health, Treatment and Medical Education, and Education, in order to develop and promote scientific, educational, research, technological, and innovation indicators in the fields of humanities, social sciences, and arts.
1-23- Developing and revising curricula
2-23- Production of educational content
3-23- Increasing the share of demand-driven theses and dissertations
4.23- Producing indigenous ideas
5-23- Job application
6-23- Domestic scholarship program for brilliant talents
7-23- Program to provide capable human resources to meet expert, administrative and managerial needs.
24- Developing a program to improve the academic level of judicial officers
25- Determining the following driving plans:
1.25- Air transport
2-25- Design, construction and production of passenger and transport aircraft
3-25- North-South transit and maritime transport corridors, railways, and north-south and east-west roads
4-25- Synergistic projects for the industry, mining and housing sectors
26- Preparing a program to stabilize prices and exchange rates at a general level and reduce inflation to single digits.
Note - The organization is required to submit a report on the actions taken regarding this article to the Parliament on a monthly basis.
Article 120-
A- The provisions of this law apply to the institutions under the supervision of the Supreme Leader (Mudhazlah al-Ali) based on His Highness' permission.
B- The regulations required by this law, in cases where no specific period for their approval is foreseen, shall be prepared within a maximum of six months from the entry into force of this law and shall be approved by the Council of Ministers. Also, the government or executive agencies, in cases where they are required to prepare and notify programs, instructions, executive packages, procedures and other matters or create digital systems but no specific period is foreseen for it, are required to prepare and approve them by the end of 1403.
C- The law regulating part of the government's financial regulations, approved on November 27, 1380, and its subsequent amendments and additions, will be enforced during the implementation of the program, and the government is required to take the necessary action within six months to determine the purpose of that law.
D- From the beginning of 1403 until the entry into force of this law, the Law of the Sixth Five-Year Plan for the Economic, Social and Cultural Development of the Islamic Republic of Iran, approved on 14/12/1395, with subsequent amendments and additions, is valid.
The above law, consisting of one hundred and twenty articles, was approved in a public session of the Islamic Consultative Assembly on Tuesday, 1/3/1403, and on 2/4/1403, the Expediency Discernment Council approved paragraph "A" of Article (11) and amended paragraph "P" and Note (2) of paragraph "C" of Article (8), paragraph "T" of Article (10), and Note (1) of paragraph "T" of Article (102) as being in accordance with the expediency of the system.
